            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ec51f3143fe04204cb3b85bbc3b311ce_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"689\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ec51f3143fe04204cb3b85bbc3b311ce_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;563&#39; height=&#39;689&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"689\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ec51f3143fe04204cb3b85bbc3b311ce_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ec51f3143fe04204cb3b85bbc3b311ce_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 令人受启发的低坐茶室<br/></p><p>前几次写到关于如何营造一个禅意满满的室内时，有幸获得一位读者的留言。他勾划出了用茶案和蒲团取代高脚四方桌椅的设想，在这样的设想背后还有希望增进人与人之间的交流，回归一种原始而真诚的生活方式的愿景。其实，对这个话题我还是很有感的，但苦于素材不够，一直都没动笔。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ca1687bbbf0562913a71f39adc3a9aa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"476\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ca1687bbbf0562913a71f39adc3a9aa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;476&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"476\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ca1687bbbf0562913a71f39adc3a9aa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ca1687bbbf0562913a71f39adc3a9aa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>说到低坐，大多数人就会联想到飘窗上的榻榻米。有没有一种可能性让低坐更大范围的走人我们的生活？</p><p>从高坐回归到低坐，关乎于<b>坐姿</b>，<b>生活方式</b>甚至是<b>心理状态</b>的改变。翻译出生的我，还带着文化对比的习惯。发现在不同文化背景下，同样是低坐，竟然携带完全不同的精神状态和文化含义。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>东方低坐</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a568dc5d7f6adffcba5e10aebd3e08b1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"479\" data-rawheight=\"606\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"479\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a568dc5d7f6adffcba5e10aebd3e08b1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;479&#39; height=&#39;606&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"479\" data-rawheight=\"606\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"479\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a568dc5d7f6adffcba5e10aebd3e08b1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a568dc5d7f6adffcba5e10aebd3e08b1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>席地而坐，就是在地上铺上筵，再在筵上垫上席，人们就跪坐在席子上。跪坐讲究的是心性内涵：通过坐姿，约束自己的道德礼仪，从而提升自身气质和品格。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a107feff892787f557f7b0d9aa1879e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"591\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a107feff892787f557f7b0d9aa1879e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;591&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"591\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a107feff892787f557f7b0d9aa1879e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0a107feff892787f557f7b0d9aa1879e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>尝试过跪坐的人都知道跪的时间长了可能会腰酸背痛，于是“凭几”应运而生。凭几是古人在席地而坐时所依靠的家具，让人坐得舒适之余而不失优雅。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f8b7a5143bc531fcfc5edf374f11728_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"360\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f8b7a5143bc531fcfc5edf374f11728_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;360&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"360\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f8b7a5143bc531fcfc5edf374f11728_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f8b7a5143bc531fcfc5edf374f11728_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>从“椅坐”回归到“跪坐”，好友之间双膝相依四目相对，身体距离与心理距离都离得很近，很容易坦诚相待相互交心。跪坐还能修养身心，安神；养腰，护膝。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-56598631a10925db2a493c9472a7e973_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"617\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-56598631a10925db2a493c9472a7e973_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;563&#39; height=&#39;617&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"617\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-56598631a10925db2a493c9472a7e973_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-56598631a10925db2a493c9472a7e973_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>跪坐有跪坐的风景。谦卑恭谨不是柔若无骨的表现，真正强大的内心才能外显谦卑和顺。日本的茶室经常设有低矮门洞或是低矮窗户，从建筑上要求来访者放低姿态，并去发现谦卑态度为人打开的别有洞天。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4bf40ad03ea3041148d8669442dd8a59_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4bf40ad03ea3041148d8669442dd8a59_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;533&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"533\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4bf40ad03ea3041148d8669442dd8a59_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-4bf40ad03ea3041148d8669442dd8a59_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果坐拥一个庭院，或者客厅是一个封闭的房间，低坐环境可以延伸至整个空间。条案最适合摆在视野空旷的窗户前。景德镇制瓷职人王建的青塘山房，用一条长案贯穿起居室，喝茶，吃饭，休憩，玩耍，成为他们一家生活的核心。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5db3b36d6a03a2070408ba3b7a125c0c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5db3b36d6a03a2070408ba3b7a125c0c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;633&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"633\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5db3b36d6a03a2070408ba3b7a125c0c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5db3b36d6a03a2070408ba3b7a125c0c_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9ee1d1c775f7f3b15b2918c2b2eb7a9b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"352\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9ee1d1c775f7f3b15b2918c2b2eb7a9b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;352&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"352\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9ee1d1c775f7f3b15b2918c2b2eb7a9b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9ee1d1c775f7f3b15b2918c2b2eb7a9b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果你的居所有个大客厅，在户型条件允许下，可以考虑把低坐区域和高坐区域相结合。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7dedfd1df9f2fc6ff36ca0ba77e3e86_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"538\" data-rawheight=\"360\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"538\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7dedfd1df9f2fc6ff36ca0ba77e3e86_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;538&#39; height=&#39;360&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"538\" data-rawheight=\"360\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"538\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7dedfd1df9f2fc6ff36ca0ba77e3e86_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a7dedfd1df9f2fc6ff36ca0ba77e3e86_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后，设一间低坐茶室可能是最多人会选择的办法。这里，我想贴心小提醒一下：茶室的装修风格如果能和其他空间风格相呼应，设计整体会更和谐。曾经看到有些朋友在很现代装饰的家中加上了一间日式茶室，风格变化很突兀，设计显得生硬。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6abfe8685460b6563826087a3eb7ff6b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1316\" data-rawheight=\"1316\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1316\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6abfe8685460b6563826087a3eb7ff6b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1316&#39; height=&#39;1316&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1316\" data-rawheight=\"1316\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1316\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6abfe8685460b6563826087a3eb7ff6b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6abfe8685460b6563826087a3eb7ff6b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>除了淘宝上各种低坐禅桌和蒲团以外，想推荐给大家“竹兰里”的茶道家具，非常具有中式风味。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>阿拉伯贝都因人(bedouin)坐式</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b7a3085242876adc77a521f0773cdd4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"901\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b7a3085242876adc77a521f0773cdd4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;800&#39; height=&#39;901&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"800\" data-rawheight=\"901\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b7a3085242876adc77a521f0773cdd4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8b7a3085242876adc77a521f0773cdd4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>说到西方低坐，你脑子里出现的肯定是这些色彩丰富，花式多样，东倒西歪在地上的垫子。这种阿拉伯国家席地而坐的方式叫贝都因人(bedouin)坐式。bedouin”在阿拉伯语中就是“荒原上的游牧民族”。由于他们游牧的生活方式，所以家具都需是便于携带。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ef460a6096beb6061e02ec3ba8bd5956_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ef460a6096beb6061e02ec3ba8bd5956_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;425&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ef460a6096beb6061e02ec3ba8bd5956_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ef460a6096beb6061e02ec3ba8bd5956_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一个典型贝都因帐篷里的场景大概就是这样吧：花花绿绿的<b>地毯</b>打底，周围堆着一圈<b>坐垫</b>可供主客一并席地而坐，中间摆放<b>茶几</b>，好茶好酒招待着。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-032581de64396f234ca8b2a860dc95a1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"695\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-032581de64396f234ca8b2a860dc95a1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;695&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"695\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-032581de64396f234ca8b2a860dc95a1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-032581de64396f234ca8b2a860dc95a1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>不同于东方人跪坐的受摄内省的<b>端庄气质</b>，贝都因人的席地而坐散发的是浪迹天涯那种随意洒脱的<b>浪漫气质</b>。<b>此两种低坐方式，一收一放，一张一驰，何不合在一起运用？</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087801914711d6c85c34b8c24b9bce58_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"618\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087801914711d6c85c34b8c24b9bce58_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;618&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"618\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087801914711d6c85c34b8c24b9bce58_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-087801914711d6c85c34b8c24b9bce58_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一起来看看如何在现代的室内运用吧！用地毯划分出整个起居空间，高坐沙发边分散堆放一些大小不一的坐垫。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d6bcf3ca7a0521fd9c784484285fd561_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d6bcf3ca7a0521fd9c784484285fd561_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d6bcf3ca7a0521fd9c784484285fd561_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d6bcf3ca7a0521fd9c784484285fd561_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>用现代淡雅的颜色来代替阿拉伯民族传统高彩布料，能让散坐区更好的和现代风格的室内融合。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-bcab608574fc85946e16777eb8332679_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"794\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-bcab608574fc85946e16777eb8332679_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;794&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"794\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-bcab608574fc85946e16777eb8332679_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-bcab608574fc85946e16777eb8332679_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>意大利的Dimore Studio在鞋店设计中运用到贝都因坐式。为了让这些波西米亚感十足的坐垫融入现代高端的环境中，设计师选用了皮质坐垫。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4c0074ac66f88f45e56cad9025ee6f2c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"742\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4c0074ac66f88f45e56cad9025ee6f2c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;742&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"742\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4c0074ac66f88f45e56cad9025ee6f2c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4c0074ac66f88f45e56cad9025ee6f2c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>由于阿拉伯民族热情好客气质的熏习，这种贝都因人坐式还适合气氛轻松随意的聚餐聚会。淘宝网店“PentFair阁楼”和“视觉味道”以波西米亚风格为主题，有兴趣的朋友可以在那里采购到异国风情的地毯和靠垫。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>现代低坐</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-06b586dddfd54d1e5c684c075cb4dcba_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"436\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"436\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-06b586dddfd54d1e5c684c075cb4dcba_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;436&#39; height=&#39;593&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"436\" data-rawheight=\"593\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"436\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-06b586dddfd54d1e5c684c075cb4dcba_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-06b586dddfd54d1e5c684c075cb4dcba_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>为了表达放松的气氛，后现代风格的沙发好多都降低了高度，和坐垫一起使用，即现代又浪漫。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69e547da8bf6ca9b898fa1b29a64feed_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69e547da8bf6ca9b898fa1b29a64feed_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1202&#39; height=&#39;1200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1202\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1202\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d91de5e817e729f49ec66379be0335d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7d91de5e817e729f49ec66379be0335d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>所有的颜色好像是被披上了一层落日的余晖，<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7108bf6008151e897f00ade89ee164c0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1196\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1196\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7108bf6008151e897f00ade89ee164c0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1196&#39; height=&#39;1200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1196\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1196\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7108bf6008151e897f00ade89ee164c0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7108bf6008151e897f00ade89ee164c0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>抑或是从海里刚刚走出来，还滴着咸滋滋的海水...<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c1d0f8e6e92a484ad952aa924717a501_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1198\" data-rawheight=\"1196\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1198\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c1d0f8e6e92a484ad952aa924717a501_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1198&#39; height=&#39;1196&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1198\" data-rawheight=\"1196\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1198\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c1d0f8e6e92a484ad952aa924717a501_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c1d0f8e6e92a484ad952aa924717a501_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这个色系不仅仅是吸引眼球的商业战略，而是以一种自然而然的方式烙在Sarah一家的生活里了。这是Sarah家的客厅，清一色的天然材料：木质书架，藤编收纳，老木桩边桌，沙发上皮草坐垫，陶器，玻璃器皿，就连书架上的书，墙上的装饰画都是大地色系。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3fe2a9471ddfe874fbd6720e5c3e9fef_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1194\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3fe2a9471ddfe874fbd6720e5c3e9fef_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1194&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1194\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3fe2a9471ddfe874fbd6720e5c3e9fef_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3fe2a9471ddfe874fbd6720e5c3e9fef_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这是她的办公/书房区域，一样的天然，简单，朴素。这样的搭配有一点是要注意的：器物简单，就越会凸显其材质和设计。仔细看看这些器物里带着精细的手工艺，和机器生产出来最终效果是不经相同的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-04032ed06d1229a2e725ae49c6e1161a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"856\" data-rawheight=\"1032\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"856\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-04032ed06d1229a2e725ae49c6e1161a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;856&#39; height=&#39;1032&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"856\" data-rawheight=\"1032\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"856\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-04032ed06d1229a2e725ae49c6e1161a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-04032ed06d1229a2e725ae49c6e1161a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>卧室里的床上用品采用亚麻或棉质布料，就喜欢这种皱皱巴巴的随意感。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fb6ad1f5d841e4471b3d5b8f29a4ef41_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"962\" data-rawheight=\"1206\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"962\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fb6ad1f5d841e4471b3d5b8f29a4ef41_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;962&#39; height=&#39;1206&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"962\" data-rawheight=\"1206\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"962\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fb6ad1f5d841e4471b3d5b8f29a4ef41_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fb6ad1f5d841e4471b3d5b8f29a4ef41_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>作为一个时尚博主，怎么能没有一个完美的试衣拍照区域呢？镜子边上的皮质灯罩可圈可点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff8e0b7b61b104583a114e93d409cfc2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1202\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1202\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff8e0b7b61b104583a114e93d409cfc2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1202&#39; height=&#39;1200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1202\" data-rawheight=\"1200\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1202\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff8e0b7b61b104583a114e93d409cfc2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ff8e0b7b61b104583a114e93d409cfc2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>摆满了货的客厅。Sarah特别喜欢vintage二手或孤品，也许这就是为什么她家那么特别的原因吧。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cc8fcb4445a456394aa4462eead8b042_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"860\" data-rawheight=\"1072\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"860\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cc8fcb4445a456394aa4462eead8b042_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;860&#39; height=&#39;1072&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"860\" data-rawheight=\"1072\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"860\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cc8fcb4445a456394aa4462eead8b042_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cc8fcb4445a456394aa4462eead8b042_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>藤编干花区域。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b1dabcf27295b5ffcb69c7113030ce75_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1068\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b1dabcf27295b5ffcb69c7113030ce75_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1068&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1068\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b1dabcf27295b5ffcb69c7113030ce75_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b1dabcf27295b5ffcb69c7113030ce75_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>宝贝们的衣着也是同样色系。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>北欧主妇大地色系之家<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8c56b304ea57350756342a0d27dd99f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"984\" data-rawheight=\"1188\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"984\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8c56b304ea57350756342a0d27dd99f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;984&#39; height=&#39;1188&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"984\" data-rawheight=\"1188\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"984\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8c56b304ea57350756342a0d27dd99f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8c56b304ea57350756342a0d27dd99f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Tessa是一位北欧的网红妈妈，和Sarah不同，她没有傲人的身材和商业头脑，从她的ins上可以看出她的生活围绕着自己的孩子和家人。和Sarah一样的是，她的生活围绕着大地色系，从家居到衣物布艺等。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b64efd0b543cbdbbd5830205641f562d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"880\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"880\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b64efd0b543cbdbbd5830205641f562d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;880&#39; height=&#39;1104&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"880\" data-rawheight=\"1104\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"880\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b64efd0b543cbdbbd5830205641f562d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b64efd0b543cbdbbd5830205641f562d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>可能是由于缺少日照的原因，北欧妈妈的大地色系比北美大陆的嬉皮风更加浓墨重彩些。明亮的黄色让人开心，深红棕色又显得低调。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-83da4aabba77c3ba62058b7057bfbbaa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"886\" data-rawheight=\"1102\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"886\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-83da4aabba77c3ba62058b7057bfbbaa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;886&#39; height=&#39;1102&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"886\" data-rawheight=\"1102\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"886\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-83da4aabba77c3ba62058b7057bfbbaa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-83da4aabba77c3ba62058b7057bfbbaa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>由于衣物都是买的同色系，随便叠完后，一摆拍都颜值很高。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e25cbbebfe0179b287f98bc60ce3e676_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"884\" data-rawheight=\"1099\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"884\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e25cbbebfe0179b287f98bc60ce3e676_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;884&#39; height=&#39;1099&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"884\" data-rawheight=\"1099\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"884\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e25cbbebfe0179b287f98bc60ce3e676_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e25cbbebfe0179b287f98bc60ce3e676_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>同样色系竟然被妈妈染到了鸡蛋壳上。在照顾家人的同时，还满足了自己的视觉美感，这样的主妇是不是做得很有成就感？<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4bf876658888ddfe5341185aa29932fa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1196\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4bf876658888ddfe5341185aa29932fa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1196&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1196\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4bf876658888ddfe5341185aa29932fa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4bf876658888ddfe5341185aa29932fa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一起来看一下她们家最受欢迎的浴室吧！北欧人的家里还是显较精致的。干净的地面和人造石浴缸无缝相接，实木小矮凳，不同色调的红陶罐，草编地毯和装饰品，白色的天然织物...最后，当然不能少了北欧人独有的外挂式收纳。色彩那么统一和谐，干外挂收纳看起来一点都不乱，而且还给空间加上些许色调。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e6c4888a055d54fe44990cb55c2ef00b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e6c4888a055d54fe44990cb55c2ef00b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1183&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1183\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e6c4888a055d54fe44990cb55c2ef00b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e6c4888a055d54fe44990cb55c2ef00b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>更多外挂收纳。这张里看到主人家里很喜欢用藤编家具和器物。不同色彩，粗细，编织方式的藤编搭配在一起，在视觉上也很令人享受。P.S.宝宝的芋头帽实在太可爱了。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-738f4099511442ea3a0f9976d288e88f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-738f4099511442ea3a0f9976d288e88f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-738f4099511442ea3a0f9976d288e88f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-738f4099511442ea3a0f9976d288e88f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>公共客厅堆满了孩子的玩具，也没有太多收纳，但是因为都是原木色，所以放在外面就像是雕塑一般。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee81c8e9593c8339c1f26c864ffda8ef_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"884\" data-rawheight=\"1106\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"884\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee81c8e9593c8339c1f26c864ffda8ef_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;884&#39; height=&#39;1106&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"884\" data-rawheight=\"1106\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"884\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee81c8e9593c8339c1f26c864ffda8ef_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee81c8e9593c8339c1f26c864ffda8ef_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>私密客厅则更多的用到了温暖的原木色。顺便一题的是，这样的日床(daybed)改成的沙发在北欧特别流行，可坐可卧，非常随意。形式上去掉了沙发厚重的靠背，而是用几个靠垫随意耷拉着，更加适合靠墙或靠角落的空间。这个办法在国内中小户型的客厅中何尝不是一种好办法呢？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7f71b3421d1010b8c48deb50a5d2471_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1114\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7f71b3421d1010b8c48deb50a5d2471_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;960&#39; height=&#39;1114&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1114\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7f71b3421d1010b8c48deb50a5d2471_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f7f71b3421d1010b8c48deb50a5d2471_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>餐厅的上空没有按常规的吊灯，而是一个随风而动的雕塑；餐桌上摆上褶皱的桌布，感觉气氛一下宁静好几个百分点。这样的家没有做太多的柜体，现代感降低，反而散发着自然清新的味道。注意餐具或是装饰瓶罐无论是色调还是精致的风格都非常统一。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-76729aa28fc2149b56b4ed9c1a25e407_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"882\" data-rawheight=\"1026\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"882\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-76729aa28fc2149b56b4ed9c1a25e407_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;882&#39; height=&#39;1026&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"882\" data-rawheight=\"1026\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"882\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-76729aa28fc2149b56b4ed9c1a25e407_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-76729aa28fc2149b56b4ed9c1a25e407_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>即使是做柜子，也是尽可能的简洁和自然。特别喜欢用洞洞作为柜门把手。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-79eb9061328372a8d8616fc9387fcaf2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1114\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-79eb9061328372a8d8616fc9387fcaf2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1114&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1114\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-79eb9061328372a8d8616fc9387fcaf2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-79eb9061328372a8d8616fc9387fcaf2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后用这张装孩子的篮子结尾，妈妈在ins上的评语是“特别喜欢孩子们新买衣服的颜色”。北欧人是多么享受生活中点点滴滴的美啊！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>总结<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d62a5f5f5d3abc308cc13ae5ec348034_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"858\" data-rawheight=\"1076\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"858\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d62a5f5f5d3abc308cc13ae5ec348034_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;858&#39; height=&#39;1076&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"858\" data-rawheight=\"1076\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"858\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d62a5f5f5d3abc308cc13ae5ec348034_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d62a5f5f5d3abc308cc13ae5ec348034_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>也许你看完这篇文章，就想跃跃欲试，把自己的家打造成一个<b>材质天然</b>，<b>层次丰富</b>的<b>大地色系</b>的家，甚至把自己的衣橱的色彩也顺便革命一下。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>小编温馨提醒一下大家，也许是因为光线，或是天气，大地色系在不同的地域散发出不同的色谱。从上面的两个案例中，我们看到即使是同样的理念，但是这两家人在对大地色系的理解上也是有差异的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>如果要找到属于中国自己的大地色系，<b>我们可以从身边的天然材料，历史古董以及蔬菜水果的颜色中吸取灵感，</b>把它们运用在家庭生活的点点滴滴中，把生活过得像一首大地色的小诗一般。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>空间|器物|仪式|心灵</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "沙之家-让时间变成一盘散沙的民宿", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ac7bbbfa717f4551ef475983bbdead0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"353\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ac7bbbfa717f4551ef475983bbdead0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;353&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"353\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ac7bbbfa717f4551ef475983bbdead0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ac7bbbfa717f4551ef475983bbdead0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>坐落于离葡萄牙首都里斯本不远的海滨城市Comporta，CASAS NA AREIA (沙之家) 就像是炎炎夏日中的一首清凉的小诗，浪漫而安静的存在着。</p><a class=\"video-box\" href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.zhihu.com/video/1138954107338465280\" target=\"_blank\" data-video-id=\"\" data-video-playable=\"true\" data-name=\"casa na areia\" data-poster=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0d2fbbdeb7aff89e4255589ca1b10fc9.jpg\" data-lens-id=\"1138954107338465280\"><img class=\"thumbnail\" src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0d2fbbdeb7aff89e4255589ca1b10fc9.jpg\"/><span class=\"content\"><span class=\"title\">casa na areia<span class=\"z-ico-extern-gray\"></span><span class=\"z-ico-extern-blue\"></span></span><span class=\"url\"><span class=\"z-ico-video\"></span>https://www.zhihu.com/video/1138954107338465280</span></span></a><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>沙之礼赞</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89253060b4f798038992d2da6e72019d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1101\" data-rawheight=\"735\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1101\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89253060b4f798038992d2da6e72019d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1101&#39; height=&#39;735&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1101\" data-rawheight=\"735\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1101\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89253060b4f798038992d2da6e72019d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89253060b4f798038992d2da6e72019d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一般意义上的家就是为了给人遮风挡雨，可是CASAS NA AREIA (沙之家) 是带你回梦乡的。建筑师Manuel Aires Mateus融合了当地传统海边渔民小屋和现代建筑元素，把现代的家具赤裸裸的放置在了一个错位的原始空间里。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-86094be79917e4335fa80a941bdccaf3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"546\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-86094be79917e4335fa80a941bdccaf3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;546&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"546\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-86094be79917e4335fa80a941bdccaf3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-86094be79917e4335fa80a941bdccaf3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>是穿越？是碰撞？还是一种似是而非的错觉？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c9a80ea162d4b85790fac67ec914425_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1101\" data-rawheight=\"735\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1101\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c9a80ea162d4b85790fac67ec914425_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1101&#39; height=&#39;735&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1101\" data-rawheight=\"735\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1101\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c9a80ea162d4b85790fac67ec914425_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-7c9a80ea162d4b85790fac67ec914425_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>边写边回想起在海边度假时那种从海里出来湿漉漉还沾满了细细的黄沙的感觉：在沙滩上丝毫没有觉得不适；可出了海滨区，如果身上还有没洗干净的沙子，就会各种不舒服。到底是沙子的错，还是我们的意识把我们的生活从原始自然和工业便利划出一道清晰的界限？<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9d70286d9344dbef8e1a4430614ab4d3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9d70286d9344dbef8e1a4430614ab4d3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;450&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"450\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9d70286d9344dbef8e1a4430614ab4d3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9d70286d9344dbef8e1a4430614ab4d3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>眼里容不了一点沙子，脚底容不下一丝污垢，也许住在沙滩上小渔屋的诗意就在于暂时把烦恼全都抛之脑后，学会和沙子共存，和即有环境共存，享受自然生活的美好。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2990953c77c5563b0c8357248f65be2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"896\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2990953c77c5563b0c8357248f65be2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;896&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"896\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2990953c77c5563b0c8357248f65be2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2990953c77c5563b0c8357248f65be2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>沙之家的主人则希望他们的客人能在这里享受到慢生活的乐趣。这一地散沙好像是千千万万个沙漏钟被砸碎而散落在地。在这里，时间似乎停止了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>沙之家<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-588eb10ad245f6e91e23acd310dce8c3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"314\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-588eb10ad245f6e91e23acd310dce8c3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;314&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"314\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-588eb10ad245f6e91e23acd310dce8c3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-588eb10ad245f6e91e23acd310dce8c3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>沙之家一共4栋房子，最多可供8个成人居住。沙之家在旺季提供整租服务，所以比较适合朋友/家庭一起度假。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8c09ca9fb6f75329ea36d505415d0234_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1418\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8c09ca9fb6f75329ea36d505415d0234_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1418&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1418\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8c09ca9fb6f75329ea36d505415d0234_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8c09ca9fb6f75329ea36d505415d0234_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>1号房：传统渔民草房。功能包括起居景观区，厨房用餐区。 沙质地面在冬天会有地暖功能，再加上南欧国家冬天气温平均10-15度。所以即使在淡季，沙之家也是很好的度假去处。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e045f1f38c800a10cdaac55341d0b12_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"766\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e045f1f38c800a10cdaac55341d0b12_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;766&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"766\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e045f1f38c800a10cdaac55341d0b12_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3e045f1f38c800a10cdaac55341d0b12_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d565599c4eccb84a770131dbb8005f5f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1074\" data-rawheight=\"748\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1074\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d565599c4eccb84a770131dbb8005f5f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;531&#39; height=&#39;341&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"531\" data-rawheight=\"341\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"531\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2db75733b8a7fbe677a72b551ccf4cba_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2db75733b8a7fbe677a72b551ccf4cba_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>4号房带有2间卧房和两个卫生间，同在一个屋檐下，最适合有小孩的一家人共同居住。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0d8e0db7430a9f7a98ce2f741a6d0324_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"756\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0d8e0db7430a9f7a98ce2f741a6d0324_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;756&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"756\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0d8e0db7430a9f7a98ce2f741a6d0324_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0d8e0db7430a9f7a98ce2f741a6d0324_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>面朝一片美丽的稻田，沙之家有一个小游泳池，在炎热的酷暑中是清凉的绿洲。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1250&#39; height=&#39;750&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1250\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1250\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6e377846d5e62253350a2ed4be8628f2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6e377846d5e62253350a2ed4be8628f2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Comporta 这个海滨城市也许对你而已只是一个陌生的外语名词，但其实在其默默无闻/朴素无华的表象之下，却被各大国际传媒机构列在各种度假胜地榜单之中。列出诸如”设计师爱你爱不够“， ”低调的星探场所“，“葡萄牙最chic的海滩”这样的评价。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8644a4df39143e1594cfdbf3d830f160_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2048\" data-rawheight=\"977\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2048\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8644a4df39143e1594cfdbf3d830f160_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1800&#39; height=&#39;1080&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1800\" data-rawheight=\"1080\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1800\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8bc4d3db2b283e25d94a7d164f9b5eb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b8bc4d3db2b283e25d94a7d164f9b5eb_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4a0360df01f2845b7f15439fd9df3c58_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1800\" data-rawheight=\"1080\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4a0360df01f2845b7f15439fd9df3c58_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
