            "title": "用情趣为自己搭一间禅意茶房", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2bd5f9e0327932b4cae2b3568358328c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"429\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2bd5f9e0327932b4cae2b3568358328c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;429&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"429\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2bd5f9e0327932b4cae2b3568358328c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2bd5f9e0327932b4cae2b3568358328c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>内心日渐憧憬东方生活画风的我，终于下定决心离开追求外在浮华的西方世界，准备要回国生活了。梦想着在新的生活空间里，能面朝庭院，设一间茶房，作为安身静心的场所。在茶房的设计中融入些许情趣，那该会是多么美好的享受啊！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>朦胧感</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ad2baa0f9e4d5f19d7ed36586cda944_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1498\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ad2baa0f9e4d5f19d7ed36586cda944_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;1498&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1498\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ad2baa0f9e4d5f19d7ed36586cda944_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5ad2baa0f9e4d5f19d7ed36586cda944_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>初见茶房时的感觉，应该是若隐若现的。犹抱琵琶半遮面，见影闻香不见其人。喝茶作为一种仪式，应该是<b>婉约的，且富有诗意的</b>。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果没有独立房间来营造茶房，则可用格栅门，隔而不断得在客厅中划出一个空间，即保持了空间的通透性，也给予客厅茶房的独立性。家人即使在不同的空间里也能互相关照到：不用言语交流，只需要感知到对方的存在即可。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae5c83e9b42f912662009365d5156ac8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae5c83e9b42f912662009365d5156ac8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;375&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae5c83e9b42f912662009365d5156ac8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae5c83e9b42f912662009365d5156ac8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>稍稍垫高基底，大约毫不费劲的一步即可。一方面，增加了空间的仪式感，比较适合低矮茶案和席地而坐的喝茶方式；另一方面，即使把隔断打开后，两个空间还了了分明。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3964dec1faacc76a9569df18b8a685e2_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"852\" data-rawheight=\"568\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"852\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3964dec1faacc76a9569df18b8a685e2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;852&#39; height=&#39;568&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"852\" data-rawheight=\"568\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"852\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3964dec1faacc76a9569df18b8a685e2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3964dec1faacc76a9569df18b8a685e2_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果把茶室设在阳台上，砌一堵中式月亮门墙作为隔断，再挂上透光的片片纱帘，夏日小风吹来，飞纱曼舞，仙气十足。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-40675430b87f333bc0c873766203fe8d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"720\" data-rawheight=\"304\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"720\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-40675430b87f333bc0c873766203fe8d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;720&#39; height=&#39;304&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"720\" data-rawheight=\"304\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"720\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-40675430b87f333bc0c873766203fe8d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-40675430b87f333bc0c873766203fe8d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>光线</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4a16f3637770eb75fb3bc46d23d37757_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"350\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"350\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;350&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"350\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"350\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4a16f3637770eb75fb3bc46d23d37757_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>幻想中最有情趣的喝茶的氛围是这样的天光，光线充足，但是却一点也不刺眼。好像江南水乡小镇的清晨，面朝河面，在屋檐下置一张茶案，当整个世界还未躁动之时，我就安安静静的在这里喝一杯茶。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cf09c6830d7a7134c07d0b235d27db56_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"742\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cf09c6830d7a7134c07d0b235d27db56_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;742&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"742\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cf09c6830d7a7134c07d0b235d27db56_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-cf09c6830d7a7134c07d0b235d27db56_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>即使居家光照环境有限，茶房也应位于窗边。窗户给人的想象力插上了翅膀。另外，自然光也比工业感极强的人造光来的更加适合喝茶这样企图和自然融为一体的仪式。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5e2f1ab5c52bf1c6aacad90be5c5c0b8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"775\" data-rawheight=\"563\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"775\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5e2f1ab5c52bf1c6aacad90be5c5c0b8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;775&#39; height=&#39;563&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"775\" data-rawheight=\"563\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"775\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5e2f1ab5c52bf1c6aacad90be5c5c0b8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5e2f1ab5c52bf1c6aacad90be5c5c0b8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果坐拥一大片窗户，会有直射光的问题，那么就要借用竹帘或素色窗帘来遮阴避暑。禅意茶房应该是<b>阴翳而内省</b>的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a0fd8213308356401c3723c35ca607c7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a0fd8213308356401c3723c35ca607c7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;461&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a0fd8213308356401c3723c35ca607c7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a0fd8213308356401c3723c35ca607c7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>清晨的第一缕阳光，或是夕阳西下，阳光在墙面勾勒出的光影也是非常迷人的。大露台上快快摆开茶席，边喝茶边品夕阳的风采。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-13472ccddb1d59f70b18348a5fa3e14e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"805\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-13472ccddb1d59f70b18348a5fa3e14e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;805&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"805\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-13472ccddb1d59f70b18348a5fa3e14e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-13472ccddb1d59f70b18348a5fa3e14e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>相比之下，如果没有自然光，就该特别注意人工灯光的营造。上面两张图同样营造若明若暗气氛，第一张的光线就显得<b>朴素清新</b>，第二张光线则更像酒吧吧台灯光。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-865d81c8063d698a5c0bc340523a4460_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-865d81c8063d698a5c0bc340523a4460_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;768&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"768\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-865d81c8063d698a5c0bc340523a4460_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-865d81c8063d698a5c0bc340523a4460_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这种新中式风格的茶室内均匀的环境光也是未尝不可的。气氛虽然没有前面明暗相间那么的私密而有趣味，但更适合招呼更多的茶友，气氛则更加公共。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中式圆</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d0ccd9656d552bac29c316ae484554f1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d0ccd9656d552bac29c316ae484554f1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;567&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"567\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d0ccd9656d552bac29c316ae484554f1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d0ccd9656d552bac29c316ae484554f1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>天圆地方是中国古人的世界观，易经、尚书等学说思想就是以此为基础的。<b>圆，取圆融，圆满之意。</b>在体现传统的人文理想的同时，也符合从古至今一脉相承，天人合一的传统美学观，圆在茶房这样富有文化含义的空间运用广泛，承载着对传统圆满精神的美好寄托。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6416232f05a71225134b3d323c9427b5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"371\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6416232f05a71225134b3d323c9427b5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;550&#39; height=&#39;371&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"371\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6416232f05a71225134b3d323c9427b5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6416232f05a71225134b3d323c9427b5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>记得在日本茶道中心一次茶道体验中，在和主人交流中也提到了圆这个概念。他认为相比中式圆的圆满，日式圆重缺陷。<br/>一国水土养育一方百姓，地理面积不足以及受到自然灾害的威胁，日本人从心理上有种忧郁气质，对于生命禅意的理解更看中短暂，脆弱，老旧等不完美的一面。从而形成了他们的侘寂美学观。它是從佛教三法印派生的概念，特別是無常。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-869ac3361f7181d1bb44929396f3af5e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-869ac3361f7181d1bb44929396f3af5e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;400&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"400\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-869ac3361f7181d1bb44929396f3af5e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-869ac3361f7181d1bb44929396f3af5e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中国自古地大物博，艺术作品中常有对崇山峻岭豪迈之情的描绘和赞叹，对于圆满的解读则是一种天人合一的精神寄托。</p><p>“天人合一”这个概念在我看来是一个非常危险的双刃剑。相信我们的初心是把有限的小我融入自然的大我的回归自然，顺应自然的道心。<b>如果不时常审视自己的内心，会不会就容易流于占有自然那份圆满的盗心？</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f298f356021658aab56f0cf414343ca8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f298f356021658aab56f0cf414343ca8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;425&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"425\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f298f356021658aab56f0cf414343ca8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f298f356021658aab56f0cf414343ca8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 中式圆和山水屏风放置在珠光宝气般的室内，显得俗气。</p><p><b>中式圆要圆得大气，也需大空间和朴素自然的环境来承接这种气场，</b>空间才会显得有中式禅味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c56316695f0ba740f323236a3f90c0d8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c56316695f0ba740f323236a3f90c0d8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;376&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c56316695f0ba740f323236a3f90c0d8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c56316695f0ba740f323236a3f90c0d8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>即使不是个整圆，却和空间大小比例非常和谐，给人一种神龙见首不见尾的感觉，好像我们所见的真相只是冰山一角罢了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-07aae30a7bcde31b0bb7a2e2ffbe3c8f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"667\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-07aae30a7bcde31b0bb7a2e2ffbe3c8f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;667&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"667\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-07aae30a7bcde31b0bb7a2e2ffbe3c8f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-07aae30a7bcde31b0bb7a2e2ffbe3c8f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>还有，如果空间不够大，小圆借景窗口会比大圆借景元素更加合适。配合盆景，以小景悟大景。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-704442ee198fa7731ca8fde31c2fedf7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-704442ee198fa7731ca8fde31c2fedf7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;423&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"423\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-704442ee198fa7731ca8fde31c2fedf7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-704442ee198fa7731ca8fde31c2fedf7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>台湾知名茶房“食养山房”的室内照片中没有传统意义上的圆的符号装饰，却用上了圆形的纸灯，不知是不是有意为之，看起来像是一轮满月，非常巧妙。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>融入自然的茶房</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dd6712c24f12f7e91315cbb993cda42_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dd6712c24f12f7e91315cbb993cda42_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;376&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dd6712c24f12f7e91315cbb993cda42_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4dd6712c24f12f7e91315cbb993cda42_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>前面提到天人合一这个概念中，如果说中式圆是这种相合的象征，那自然则是天，是道。可恰恰在现代都市，能时时刻刻亲近大自然变成了一种奢侈。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-80f0336f7e554b3ffcf268ee2342edf4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-80f0336f7e554b3ffcf268ee2342edf4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;625&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"625\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-80f0336f7e554b3ffcf268ee2342edf4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-80f0336f7e554b3ffcf268ee2342edf4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>从古至今，无论中式日式，茶和自然关系都是无缝的。日式茶房跪坐在室内，面朝庭院，屋内也注意摆放插花。通过约束和仪式感，受摄处于尘世中散乱内心。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3d36fbe6a7f10af790643aea7d35bbb7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1500\" data-rawheight=\"1967\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3d36fbe6a7f10af790643aea7d35bbb7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1500&#39; height=&#39;1967&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1500\" data-rawheight=\"1967\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3d36fbe6a7f10af790643aea7d35bbb7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3d36fbe6a7f10af790643aea7d35bbb7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 圃生的国画</p><p>圃生的国画中描绘出古人隐居在山中屋前小院以树墩为案，树荫为檐，山林中鸟叫为轻音乐，读书喝茶好不乐乎。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10572214b307709a149d385d0b1de773_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1300\" data-rawheight=\"866\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1300\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10572214b307709a149d385d0b1de773_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1300&#39; height=&#39;866&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1300\" data-rawheight=\"866\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1300\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10572214b307709a149d385d0b1de773_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10572214b307709a149d385d0b1de773_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中国建筑大师董豫赣耳里庭客舍营造出屋前小院，上有绿树遮阴避暑，搭张竹席，一家人围坐，喝茶，吃零食水果，自在而休闲。真正生活在自然中，则无需受摄，而是顺应自然。</p><p>中日两种茶道，个人认为是没有高低上下的。而是因人而异，对症下药而已。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61e54f69c014eca7afd9b6d14c1eb2e0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61e54f69c014eca7afd9b6d14c1eb2e0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;375&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61e54f69c014eca7afd9b6d14c1eb2e0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61e54f69c014eca7afd9b6d14c1eb2e0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果生活在都市里条件有限，没有太多的阳台空间，在茶房室内摆上三五植物，盆景，或插花都很给空间气氛加分。也许这就是最廉价的奢侈了吧。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-256abfa06513ef1d41d6cf317065ffb6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"416\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-256abfa06513ef1d41d6cf317065ffb6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;690&#39; height=&#39;416&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"690\" data-rawheight=\"416\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"690\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-256abfa06513ef1d41d6cf317065ffb6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-256abfa06513ef1d41d6cf317065ffb6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后，以网上找到的这群有着诗情画意的禅茶修行人来结尾。一切情趣都只不过是手段，最终归不归心才是最重要的。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>空间|器物|仪式|心灵</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "如何营造一个禅意满满的家 - 银色金属", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd27ee8fe010e67096dc57488b8a67d1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd27ee8fe010e67096dc57488b8a67d1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;960&#39; height=&#39;1199&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd27ee8fe010e67096dc57488b8a67d1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd27ee8fe010e67096dc57488b8a67d1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>让我第一次把金属和禅意联系在一起的还要数安邸杂志上的这个乡村私宅的案例：磨砂铝合金表面反射着柔和的光，在一幅堆满东方元素的布景中给人一种耐人寻味的错位感。我搞不清这幅画面到底是北京还是纽约？到底是东方，还是西方？虽然中式室内并没有大面积使用金属的传统，但是这里的风景禅意悠悠，铝合金柜的布景丝毫没有违和感，反而给画面中的材质增加了些层次感：金属表面的光滑对应着假山石的粗糙，金属的肃杀感对应着木材的生发感，最后绿枝和黄杏点缀点睛，整幅画面令人向往。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a5268396df69597fdadf756a48f00546_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a5268396df69597fdadf756a48f00546_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a5268396df69597fdadf756a48f00546_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a5268396df69597fdadf756a48f00546_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>以前曾经写过的一个光线涂色的家的案例，主人搜集的一个古董银质水壶在阳光下闪着柔美而圣洁的光。西方宗教建筑中，对于光线的营造尤其重要，因为它代表着神的踪影。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3fe178bfcb1f0d7f871b5a7d776ee91_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"440\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"440\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3fe178bfcb1f0d7f871b5a7d776ee91_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;440&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"440\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"440\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3fe178bfcb1f0d7f871b5a7d776ee91_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3fe178bfcb1f0d7f871b5a7d776ee91_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>而在东方文化里，金属神性不太在于其反射之光，而更是其反射之象。古时铜镜，反射之象朦朦胧胧，虚实真假。红楼梦中的“风月宝鉴”镜，正面照出美女，反面照出骷髅，正反两面反映了事物现象和本质。<b>镜花水月，到万境归空，人世到头时，发现一切不过一场大梦。而金属的镜面似乎是通向另一个世界的大门。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6a6a7d95a80235fc631fc19f228f623_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"848\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6a6a7d95a80235fc631fc19f228f623_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;848&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"848\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6a6a7d95a80235fc631fc19f228f623_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d6a6a7d95a80235fc631fc19f228f623_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>磨得蹭亮的金属表面形成镜面效果。置身自然之中，建筑无我的反射着自然，建筑就变成了自然。好似一个得道仙人，金属静静的跟大家诉说着“<b>放空自我，你便是整个宇宙</b>“的道理。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6662c6551220fbd99b487d6e239c1127_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6662c6551220fbd99b487d6e239c1127_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;752&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6662c6551220fbd99b487d6e239c1127_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-6662c6551220fbd99b487d6e239c1127_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中国传统五行里金元素蕴含着沉降，肃杀，收敛的意象，和极简主义那种剔除繁复，回归本源的理念不谋而合。而上图中的铝合金材质完美营造了极简风格的时装工作室空间。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1d161121a8f2db55644cf9a2a8179a6e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1222\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1d161121a8f2db55644cf9a2a8179a6e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;1222&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"1222\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1d161121a8f2db55644cf9a2a8179a6e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1d161121a8f2db55644cf9a2a8179a6e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>相比近年来国内非常流行的贵气十足的黄铜，银色的金属显得更加脱俗，前卫。东方感十足的空间内运用酷酷的铝合金材质，一下把古老的文明穿越到了未来。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-306becd4acd3f717d1bf94729337553d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-306becd4acd3f717d1bf94729337553d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-306becd4acd3f717d1bf94729337553d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-306becd4acd3f717d1bf94729337553d_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1909984960b18659ebd6f8438f67078e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1440\" data-rawheight=\"1917\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1440\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1909984960b18659ebd6f8438f67078e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1440&#39; height=&#39;1917&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1440\" data-rawheight=\"1917\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1440\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1909984960b18659ebd6f8438f67078e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1909984960b18659ebd6f8438f67078e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>看了前面那么些图，细心的你可能会发现，金属表面大面积使用会让空间变得冷酷而不近人情，更适合商业空间，不够适合住宅空间。丹麦著名家具品牌Frama擅长在其极简住宅空间中小面积的点缀铝合金材质家具。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-101906591d38202fd08484d71ff9d753_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"922\" data-rawheight=\"888\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"922\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-101906591d38202fd08484d71ff9d753_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;922&#39; height=&#39;888&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"922\" data-rawheight=\"888\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"922\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-101906591d38202fd08484d71ff9d753_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-101906591d38202fd08484d71ff9d753_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>上图这款Triangolo Chair是1989年设计的，至今风采依然。采用钢材质，几何元素配上极简线条，售价1050欧元。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b0e7e5d910c4e8cbcb1ec0acebec8532_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2280\" data-rawheight=\"1278\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2280\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b0e7e5d910c4e8cbcb1ec0acebec8532_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2280&#39; height=&#39;1278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2280\" data-rawheight=\"1278\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2280\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b0e7e5d910c4e8cbcb1ec0acebec8532_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b0e7e5d910c4e8cbcb1ec0acebec8532_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>古董商兼著名纽约室内设计师 Ferrer Charlie也偏爱用银色金属小件家具点缀室内，上面作品里用到的椅子是上个世纪50年代设计师Pierre Guariche的作品 &#34;Tonneau&#34; 的铸铝版本。作为古董，大家可以在网上不同卖家手上买到新旧程度/价格不同的二手货。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-75b7ce5f947a1b4f4ed05f374bca5966_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"432\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"432\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-75b7ce5f947a1b4f4ed05f374bca5966_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;432&#39; height=&#39;666&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"432\" data-rawheight=\"666\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"432\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-75b7ce5f947a1b4f4ed05f374bca5966_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-75b7ce5f947a1b4f4ed05f374bca5966_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中国艺术家邵帆的不锈钢材质的圈椅融合了传统和现代，东方和西方。作为艺术品，同时也是家具，可供使用，也可供收藏。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-404b7d24bc13987d1403cd040b70cb7c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1110\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-404b7d24bc13987d1403cd040b70cb7c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;1110&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"1110\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-404b7d24bc13987d1403cd040b70cb7c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-404b7d24bc13987d1403cd040b70cb7c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Frama家对银色金属点缀家居非常钟爱，还研发铝制边桌Rivet Side Table/Rivet Box Table。组装方式设计感极强：由于铝材质柔软而不容易焊接或使用螺钉连接，这款边桌运用了中国传统的铆榫技术来连接不同的组建。每个边桌500欧元左右价格。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-01ce59fd70017d67c2d568e0359d9030_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1446\" data-rawheight=\"1152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1446\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-01ce59fd70017d67c2d568e0359d9030_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1446&#39; height=&#39;1152&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1446\" data-rawheight=\"1152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1446\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-01ce59fd70017d67c2d568e0359d9030_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-01ce59fd70017d67c2d568e0359d9030_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>摆放在极简风格的客厅，非常应情应景。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-46ebbee4ac520b81e78baf24ddd85ac9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"798\" data-rawheight=\"1197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"798\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-46ebbee4ac520b81e78baf24ddd85ac9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;798&#39; height=&#39;1197&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"798\" data-rawheight=\"1197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"798\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-46ebbee4ac520b81e78baf24ddd85ac9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-46ebbee4ac520b81e78baf24ddd85ac9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>钟爱极简主义风格的法国建筑师Joseph Dirand在巴黎自家公寓使用了镜面金属茶几，成为整个空间的亮点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3e1303b09a35a990b000d29305527f9f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"1174\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3e1303b09a35a990b000d29305527f9f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;768&#39; height=&#39;1174&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"1174\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3e1303b09a35a990b000d29305527f9f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3e1303b09a35a990b000d29305527f9f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>由于便于清洁以及和洁白的陶瓷制品搭配无缝隙，银色金属也是厨房装饰神器。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-564c023fc98e9c4cec5c2562d049d3c8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2620\" data-rawheight=\"1026\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2620\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-564c023fc98e9c4cec5c2562d049d3c8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2620&#39; height=&#39;1026&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2620\" data-rawheight=\"1026\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2620\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-564c023fc98e9c4cec5c2562d049d3c8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-564c023fc98e9c4cec5c2562d049d3c8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Frama的Rivet Case 可横可竖，适合放在客厅的餐桌边上。价格1500欧元左右。</p><p>Rivet Shelf 每个500欧元左右。可以安装在客厅或是厨房的墙面上。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bcb288716798beda818c1ba4bb891300_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bcb288716798beda818c1ba4bb891300_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;375&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bcb288716798beda818c1ba4bb891300_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bcb288716798beda818c1ba4bb891300_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>别墅的厨房有足够的空间，可以尝试不锈钢中岛。当然，请注意搭配不同材质，比如上图运用斑驳砖块老墙，黑色木质组柜和浅木质地板，使空间材质的层次丰富起来。如果过多使用不锈钢，自家厨房弄不好看起来就会像餐馆厨房。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c3f8aaafd69a56877de86fc4944c6ca_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c3f8aaafd69a56877de86fc4944c6ca_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;705&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c3f8aaafd69a56877de86fc4944c6ca_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c3f8aaafd69a56877de86fc4944c6ca_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后，如果你有足够的功力，可以挑战在家中更大面积使用金属表面。比如上面这个空间，用铝板材做成了柜门，成为墙体表面。一方面给空间引入了更多柔和的光线(由于金属反射光的左右)，另一方面和一旁圆窗和背景木格门这般中式元素互相作用，营造比较另类的禅味。</p><p>唯一本人不太赞同的就是金属墙前面的仙人掌雕塑，虽然颜色搭配上和空间非常融合，但却给人一种冰冻沙漠的意象，让空间显得更加冰冷和孤独。家的感觉应该是舒适自然，加点绿植让它恢复生机和希望吧！<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>空间|器物|仪式|心灵</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;746&#39; height=&#39;746&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f1b0f6d1c1cdba61dab4c7f25b0c3cc3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"344\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"344\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;344&#39; height=&#39;344&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"344\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"344\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f1b0f6d1c1cdba61dab4c7f25b0c3cc3_b.jpg\"/></figure>",

            "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/72537482", 
            "userName": "治愈家杂志", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/d97614d3497ec610467aec3d7ae89f53", 
            "upvote": 1, 
            "title": "如何营造一个禅意满满的家-色调篇", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4adaac79be7f3859a3c024d8de4d2af6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1191\" data-rawheight=\"785\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1191\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4adaac79be7f3859a3c024d8de4d2af6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1191&#39; height=&#39;785&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1191\" data-rawheight=\"785\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1191\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4adaac79be7f3859a3c024d8de4d2af6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4adaac79be7f3859a3c024d8de4d2af6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>什么是一个禅意空间？让人放慢脚步，思维清空，最终起到身心放松和治愈的功能的空间都应该带着禅的种子。</p><p>上一期介绍了天然泥灰类(plaster)室内涂料,通过那种不规则，老旧和寂灭感来营造那种“逝者如斯”的悠悠禅意。事实上，不用泥灰涂料，如果用对了色调和注意空间留白，禅意一样能被营造出来。</p><p>纵观世界不同地区，禅的意境通过不同的文化性格，示现出不同的样貌。这一期我们就来一起试图探讨一下不同文化背景所营造禅意空间的色调。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d73eb58f431ced3b61550d7b0c6c4d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>二十世纪极简主义</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e81cf57d48792e13d967b778480e69f8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e81cf57d48792e13d967b778480e69f8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;394&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"394\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e81cf57d48792e13d967b778480e69f8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e81cf57d48792e13d967b778480e69f8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>崇尚“少即是多”的西方极简主义和东方禅意有着异曲同工之妙。现代建筑大师密斯·凡德罗认为建筑是一种语言，如果能把不必要的元素剔除再剔除，那精炼后的空间就能成为一首诗，意味深远，令人品后口齿留香。东方禅修通过静坐法门去除杂念，一层层深入自我的本来面目，直至明心见性。</p><p>这其中的“少”并不是真正的少，而是去除糟粕后进一步去品细微中的美；而“多”则指的是当你真正打开那扇隐形的大门后，发现原来浮在表面的只是冰山一角。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-12d1c212993480dcefc8cfb4d5866c47_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-12d1c212993480dcefc8cfb4d5866c47_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-12d1c212993480dcefc8cfb4d5866c47_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-12d1c212993480dcefc8cfb4d5866c47_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>比如这张洁白的棉花糖照片，经过提炼后，同样的白色在不同位置受到不同光线的作用，反映出不同调子的白色(右边色块)。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-94b9eeef1d278efeb13fadcacb94a82d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-94b9eeef1d278efeb13fadcacb94a82d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;563&#39; height=&#39;687&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"687\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-94b9eeef1d278efeb13fadcacb94a82d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-94b9eeef1d278efeb13fadcacb94a82d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>同样，看上去一片白色的极简风格室内，细细观察后，发现墙壁，地板，地毯，窗帘，吧台的白色又不尽相同。设计师刻意运用不同材质和不同调子的白色，营造出不同层次，令空间显得宁静且不乏味。<br/><b>极简主义风格配色善于从平凡/朴素的中性色系中提炼出有趣而细腻的色彩搭配，并且善用材料天然纹理来增加颜色的层次感。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e88088c1f1452084a889900636314d7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"984\" data-rawheight=\"176\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"984\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e88088c1f1452084a889900636314d7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;984&#39; height=&#39;176&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"984\" data-rawheight=\"176\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"984\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e88088c1f1452084a889900636314d7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e88088c1f1452084a889900636314d7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中性色又称为无彩色，基色由黑白灰，卡其色，咖啡色组成。中性色在上世纪50年被中古风格拥抱，直至今日流行未减，可谓是“不会错”的选择。原因其一，中性色调性中庸，即使大多数人不喜欢也不会太讨厌；其二是这些颜色无论是搭配在一起或是和其他鲜艳的色彩搭配都不会有违和感。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-442996eeee28b2f017157ffb8b9a8a3a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"537\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-442996eeee28b2f017157ffb8b9a8a3a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;537&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"537\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-442996eeee28b2f017157ffb8b9a8a3a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-442996eeee28b2f017157ffb8b9a8a3a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>上图这个空间整体采用了棕灰色为主色调，灵星点缀配上纹理丰富的深棕色的门和几。地板灰色和高脚餐桌相呼应。整体色彩<b>调和</b>，清爽而古朴。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-856e460cc96d4bd6f638ae7580c114a6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"818\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-856e460cc96d4bd6f638ae7580c114a6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;818&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"818\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-856e460cc96d4bd6f638ae7580c114a6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-856e460cc96d4bd6f638ae7580c114a6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这个餐厅用了现代都市感极强的黑色和不同灰色调子为主色，和前一个例子不同的是，为了中和灰黑冷酷的感觉，设计中加入了原木材质的椅子，一亮一暗，形成<b>对比色</b>，空间也显得活泼起来。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>北欧设计的中庸之道</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6d2a64b90800488487a7ef0d39b11f69_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1079\" data-rawheight=\"753\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1079\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6d2a64b90800488487a7ef0d39b11f69_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1079&#39; height=&#39;753&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1079\" data-rawheight=\"753\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1079\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6d2a64b90800488487a7ef0d39b11f69_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6d2a64b90800488487a7ef0d39b11f69_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>极简主义的美学需要怀着断舍离的心境后才能细细品味，而北欧的美学观“lagom”则更加有人情味：这是一种追求适当、平衡的生活方式：不要太多，也不要太少，刚刚好才是最好。北欧设计相比美国盛行的极简风，融入了更多的色彩，而禅意丝毫不减。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f9099dd1d0860c7a19db8c1eef158186_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"438\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f9099dd1d0860c7a19db8c1eef158186_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;438&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"438\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f9099dd1d0860c7a19db8c1eef158186_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f9099dd1d0860c7a19db8c1eef158186_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>北欧室内墙面涂料色彩让我联想到了近年来国人非常追捧的莫兰迪色系。莫兰迪是上世纪意大利一位静物画画家。<b>他用低纯度低饱和度色彩诠释的日用器物，好像被时光披上了一层外衣。</b><br/></p><p>有意思的是，莫兰迪是当时一位非常与众不同的隐士画家。在那个人人标榜个性与标新立异的时代，莫兰迪的作品与世无争，弥散着一股操着异国口音的禅味。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9fa327f281ce1e64f898f9036786e103_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"749\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9fa327f281ce1e64f898f9036786e103_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;749&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"749\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9fa327f281ce1e64f898f9036786e103_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9fa327f281ce1e64f898f9036786e103_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8a9b9e996125efcdf1074ff4f06dd08c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2672\" data-rawheight=\"1875\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2672\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8a9b9e996125efcdf1074ff4f06dd08c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2672&#39; height=&#39;1875&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2672\" data-rawheight=\"1875\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2672\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8a9b9e996125efcdf1074ff4f06dd08c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8a9b9e996125efcdf1074ff4f06dd08c_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-358beab9de95e94686bad580a8a4bd01_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-358beab9de95e94686bad580a8a4bd01_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;958&#39; height=&#39;556&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"958\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"958\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-358beab9de95e94686bad580a8a4bd01_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-358beab9de95e94686bad580a8a4bd01_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>上面这三幅莫兰迪的作品对应的室内分别是北欧著名涂料品牌佐敦涂料(Jotun)效果图和北欧禅意大师Axel Vervoordt的作品。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36db064399bfe7793948d7132570b21c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1002\" data-rawheight=\"667\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36db064399bfe7793948d7132570b21c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1002&#39; height=&#39;667&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1002\" data-rawheight=\"667\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36db064399bfe7793948d7132570b21c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36db064399bfe7793948d7132570b21c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>以前的文章中曾经介绍过佐敦涂料(Jotun)，他家的中性色高雅中透着人情味；其他冷暖色的纯度、饱和度都偏低，暗合了莫兰迪的用色特点。下面这几幅用色相对鲜艳，禅味还在。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-212c59534d017bc421053787ca1e2c9d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"760\" data-rawheight=\"988\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"760\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-212c59534d017bc421053787ca1e2c9d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;760&#39; height=&#39;988&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"760\" data-rawheight=\"988\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"760\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-212c59534d017bc421053787ca1e2c9d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-212c59534d017bc421053787ca1e2c9d_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7939bda29a707912ccb959a1b3859c22_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"1152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7939bda29a707912ccb959a1b3859c22_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;768&#39; height=&#39;1152&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"1152\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7939bda29a707912ccb959a1b3859c22_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7939bda29a707912ccb959a1b3859c22_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bdfa23a7b28c3a2b98f2e16412daa977_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"1182\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bdfa23a7b28c3a2b98f2e16412daa977_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;1182&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"1182\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bdfa23a7b28c3a2b98f2e16412daa977_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bdfa23a7b28c3a2b98f2e16412daa977_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>东方禅境之色</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f5762266cc841f32cc44a1df7aa17a8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1800\" data-rawheight=\"1201\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f5762266cc841f32cc44a1df7aa17a8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1800&#39; height=&#39;1201&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1800\" data-rawheight=\"1201\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1800\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f5762266cc841f32cc44a1df7aa17a8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f5762266cc841f32cc44a1df7aa17a8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 中式禅茶室</p><p>最后再来回眸一望我们自己的东方文化。如果说西方人热情直接，那东方人则含蓄内敛；西方人勤于改造外在世界，求新求变，东方人则喜好追求内在的圆满和永恒；西方的现代建筑注重运用新材料，新技术，东方建筑则偏向自然而注重意境，材料方面以木为主。色彩可清新淡雅，亦可老成稳重。一般建筑是这样，更加注重留白的禅意空间亦如此。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-143f93adc223305b6e64a3f384090524_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-143f93adc223305b6e64a3f384090524_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;370&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"370\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-143f93adc223305b6e64a3f384090524_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-143f93adc223305b6e64a3f384090524_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;525&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"525\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d78f02288cce09f353209184b0e12220_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>大道至简，中国传统建筑用木材这一个简单的材料，和阴阳虚实的手法，营造出千变万化的内在建筑空间。而东方禅意空间的颜色就像是一幅用木头打起来的水墨画。</b>正如道德经里所著：道生一，一生二，二生三，三生万物。把木头切条切块后再拼制起来，可做屏风也可做窗格。透和不透之间引导人从物质世界进入意识境界。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2548705b9e0ccd94dad692819f73c561_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1704\" data-rawheight=\"1136\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1704\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2548705b9e0ccd94dad692819f73c561_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1704&#39; height=&#39;1136&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1704\" data-rawheight=\"1136\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1704\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2548705b9e0ccd94dad692819f73c561_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2548705b9e0ccd94dad692819f73c561_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>阴阳虚实观也同样可以运用在室内和室外的关系上。<b>自然本身就是最好的装饰：色，香，声，味俱全，还能养神悟道，所以要通过借景，把它们引入室内。</b>如果有条件能够坐拥一个院子，即使再小，也要精心营造。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-78461a581453fe4a87b2cf8fbf36aa12_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-78461a581453fe4a87b2cf8fbf36aa12_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;563&#39; height=&#39;375&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"375\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-78461a581453fe4a87b2cf8fbf36aa12_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-78461a581453fe4a87b2cf8fbf36aa12_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>即使窗外一片高楼大厦或是市井街巷，在屋内养些形态各异的盆景，透过一丝绿意，真理也能以小见大。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6cd0864e11eac8a8fa3f18072b5c5530_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"798\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6cd0864e11eac8a8fa3f18072b5c5530_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;563&#39; height=&#39;798&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"563\" data-rawheight=\"798\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"563\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6cd0864e11eac8a8fa3f18072b5c5530_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6cd0864e11eac8a8fa3f18072b5c5530_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>日式禅境则喜欢摆放些枯枝，中式茶房多喜引入枯枝老木作为茶桌，象征着永恒的寂灭和岁月的张力，禅味更加简单粗暴。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-78d1786cba6756503799dbc694ab5607_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"380\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-78d1786cba6756503799dbc694ab5607_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;640&#39; height=&#39;380&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"640\" data-rawheight=\"380\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"640\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-78d1786cba6756503799dbc694ab5607_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-78d1786cba6756503799dbc694ab5607_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后，光线也是室内色彩的很重要的组成部分。<b>东方禅境阴翳内省</b>。一般空间也不喜阳光直射而喜间接光。禅房则更加，从角落射入的一线阳光似乎象征着世间烦恼困顿中的一丝解脱。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d7c085b9a436b54bdc863d5dc36ade7d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"424\" data-rawheight=\"573\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"424\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d7c085b9a436b54bdc863d5dc36ade7d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;424&#39; height=&#39;573&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"424\" data-rawheight=\"573\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"424\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d7c085b9a436b54bdc863d5dc36ade7d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d7c085b9a436b54bdc863d5dc36ade7d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>哪种禅的颜色和你的禅心相合？<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>空间|器物|仪式|心灵</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;746&#39; height=&#39;746&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"746\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"746\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-08f66b063f3f2d13c2940d2f4627cbea_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-f1b0f6d1c1cdba61dab4c7f25b0c3cc3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"344\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"344\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
