            "upvote": 1, 
            "title": "复古禅意空间墙面涂料㊙️方", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf7bbd7ddd34a62447ffdd5c84ff0849_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"353\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf7bbd7ddd34a62447ffdd5c84ff0849_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;353&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"353\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf7bbd7ddd34a62447ffdd5c84ff0849_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf7bbd7ddd34a62447ffdd5c84ff0849_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>要布置一个有禅意的治愈家，得力的墙面涂料是一剂杀手锏。就像室内空间的衣服一样，不同颜色和质地的墙面涂料能赋予空间不同的性格。今天要介绍的性感材料健康，时尚，但是可能还真有点贵。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;733&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实已经好久想给大家介绍<b>limewash (室内石灰涂料)</b>这个涂料了，但是我真的犹豫了好久。因为这个涂料在国外非常受人追捧，但是国内竟然几乎没有任何报道。在网上找了半天，也只找到了一两家品牌的经销商，非常令人不解。看完文章，可能你才会了解其中究竟。<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0af33fbbb532ad5711e689bee161da3f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0af33fbbb532ad5711e689bee161da3f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0af33fbbb532ad5711e689bee161da3f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0af33fbbb532ad5711e689bee161da3f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>石灰涂料是一种可以追溯到罗马时代的古老涂料，涂料的基础材料是石灰与水混合制成的石灰腻子，并用天然色素着色。石灰涂料是以矿物质为原料，是非常天然环保的一款高端涂料。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6f5b4c455dd47ee5a546eb5574c84b29_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"842\" data-rawheight=\"806\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"842\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6f5b4c455dd47ee5a546eb5574c84b29_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;842&#39; height=&#39;806&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"842\" data-rawheight=\"806\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"842\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6f5b4c455dd47ee5a546eb5574c84b29_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6f5b4c455dd47ee5a546eb5574c84b29_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>Limewash(石灰涂料)能创造出有淡淡纹理的哑光表面。和国内市场上类似质地的“清水混凝土漆”相比，石灰涂料有种粉笔质感的绒面效果。同样是冷色，石灰涂料比清水混凝土漆显得更加温暖，透着低调的豪华。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-14a315b32567491ba748213b6fa27065_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-14a315b32567491ba748213b6fa27065_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;733&#39; height=&#39;458&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"458\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-14a315b32567491ba748213b6fa27065_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-14a315b32567491ba748213b6fa27065_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>比利时wabi sabi室内设计大师Axel Vervoordt可是运用Limewash(石灰涂料)的老手。一方面由于比利时一直保留着使用石灰涂料的传统；另一方面，这样的墙面对于他特别擅长的充满光阴感的室内非常相得益彰。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-21e40e22baba4739899bd604ebbf2b8c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1270\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1270\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-21e40e22baba4739899bd604ebbf2b8c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1270&#39; height=&#39;800&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1270\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1270\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-21e40e22baba4739899bd604ebbf2b8c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-21e40e22baba4739899bd604ebbf2b8c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>左图中Axel Vervoordt用石灰涂料所营造的那种老旧感完全和江南粉墙黛瓦是同一个画风。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe98a93686d6fe82291aff611ed72d73_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe98a93686d6fe82291aff611ed72d73_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe98a93686d6fe82291aff611ed72d73_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fe98a93686d6fe82291aff611ed72d73_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>和乳胶漆相比，石灰涂料的基础材料是石灰和天然色素，没有那些有毒的添加剂。改良版的室内石灰涂料中添加了些矿物质的粘合剂，使石灰涂料尽可能得去适应现代人的生活环境，同时也保证产品的天然/环保性能。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d533d96db5a752751ccc29baeedf5df5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"743\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d533d96db5a752751ccc29baeedf5df5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;700&#39; height=&#39;743&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"700\" data-rawheight=\"743\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"700\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d533d96db5a752751ccc29baeedf5df5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d533d96db5a752751ccc29baeedf5df5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>石灰的高ph值使得微生物无法存活，以及石灰本身带有细微小孔的特质，使得涂有石灰涂料的室内能够和户外进行呼吸，有<b>优化室内空气质量的功能。</b><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>另外，石灰涂料和一般涂料另一个不同点是，一般涂料只附着于墙面表层，石灰涂料会滲透入墙体，所以最佳附着表面是多孔材料，比如石膏，砖块或石头，这样石灰才能牢牢抓住表面，和其融为一体。<b>选购石灰涂料时一定要向经销商询问需不需要购买底漆，让石灰涂料更好的适应现代住宅毛坯墙面。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da2f1bfd0831b8724b635de2b980330b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da2f1bfd0831b8724b635de2b980330b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da2f1bfd0831b8724b635de2b980330b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da2f1bfd0831b8724b635de2b980330b_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cfae3ad210e5dc48bde22f8d19a1d281_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1838\" data-rawheight=\"1022\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1838\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cfae3ad210e5dc48bde22f8d19a1d281_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1838&#39; height=&#39;1022&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1838\" data-rawheight=\"1022\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1838\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cfae3ad210e5dc48bde22f8d19a1d281_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cfae3ad210e5dc48bde22f8d19a1d281_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>石灰涂料最有意思的点就是它最终呈现的颜色比较任性。石灰涂料<b>干了以后颜色几乎会比湿的时候浅10倍</b>。请看上面上石灰涂料的过程：</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>1.涂第一遍湿时的视觉效果</p><p>2.第一遍干了后开始涂第二层</p><p>3.第二遍刚刚涂完</p><p>4.第二遍干后的样子（屋内光线比较强，看起来偏亮）</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>是不是有点受骗上当的感觉，涂了半天感觉还好像没涂似的。所以在上墙之前小面积的-<b>试-颜-色</b>！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f617e3b3fb6ebf2a7c6c116504cec535_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f617e3b3fb6ebf2a7c6c116504cec535_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1200&#39; height=&#39;1000&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f617e3b3fb6ebf2a7c6c116504cec535_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f617e3b3fb6ebf2a7c6c116504cec535_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>上面这些都是试色色卡，颜色深浅度取决于所涂覆的涂层数量。一般来说可涂三层，但也取决于不同涂料。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bcdd6508975f099d194a42261873b3e7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bcdd6508975f099d194a42261873b3e7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bcdd6508975f099d194a42261873b3e7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bcdd6508975f099d194a42261873b3e7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这是我上学时色彩选修课的石灰涂料课留影。右图中大家可以看到用吹风机吹干的部分的颜色比还湿着的地方要浅好多呢。另外，由于色素都是采用天然矿物质，所以石灰涂料可以提供的色彩其实很有限。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9bac632588e1439ad18000c03a1483bc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"488\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9bac632588e1439ad18000c03a1483bc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;733&#39; height=&#39;488&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"488\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9bac632588e1439ad18000c03a1483bc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9bac632588e1439ad18000c03a1483bc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>为了达到那种斑驳的阴影效果，石灰涂料必配这样粗毛的石灰涂料刷，并且刷时得左右来回刷，造成斑驳肌理。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ad953bcb9940f9ba25cca18cc765540_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ad953bcb9940f9ba25cca18cc765540_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;746&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"746\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ad953bcb9940f9ba25cca18cc765540_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6ad953bcb9940f9ba25cca18cc765540_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36802508675748aa70eb3ebfcfaa22ac_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36802508675748aa70eb3ebfcfaa22ac_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36802508675748aa70eb3ebfcfaa22ac_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-36802508675748aa70eb3ebfcfaa22ac_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;733&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"733\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"733\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2770b6e04ed4aea8b4ebd1b16e045349_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>给大家介绍一下几个做limewash石灰涂料的国际品牌：</p><p>1.美国品牌Sydney Harbour Paint Company的Interno Lime Wash这款适用于室内。</p><p>2.BioPittura是一个经典的石灰涂料品牌，室内外都适合使用。 </p><p>3.瑞典品牌Kalklitir Natural Lime Wash。</p><p>4.澳大利亚品牌Bauwerk Colour的石灰涂料色彩非常艳丽好看（上图红砖色的墙面就是他们家的产品）。</p><p>5.<b>法国品牌Nature et Harmonie®室内石灰涂料在国内有代理销售。</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a97e8d52ec4f446d0050351e3b0d376f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a97e8d52ec4f446d0050351e3b0d376f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a97e8d52ec4f446d0050351e3b0d376f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a97e8d52ec4f446d0050351e3b0d376f_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66138f87bf3b3699cd032487333a7dca_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"847\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66138f87bf3b3699cd032487333a7dca_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;847&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"847\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66138f87bf3b3699cd032487333a7dca_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66138f87bf3b3699cd032487333a7dca_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>石灰涂墙一般<b>不推荐经常清洁</b>，其实也不需要，由于石灰涂料斑驳的阴影效果有隐藏污渍的效果。如果真的需要清洁，一般只需重涂上一层稀释石灰涂料就可以了。这样的清洁方式可能真的比较适合大而空的乡下老宅吧～<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-90ff473e3b2c722764bdeced627d127c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-90ff473e3b2c722764bdeced627d127c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-90ff473e3b2c722764bdeced627d127c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-90ff473e3b2c722764bdeced627d127c_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0792aac66037b37c42eb03ca909bbcfc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"487\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0792aac66037b37c42eb03ca909bbcfc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;650&#39; height=&#39;487&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"487\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0792aac66037b37c42eb03ca909bbcfc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0792aac66037b37c42eb03ca909bbcfc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>优点：</b></p><ul><li>会呼吸的涂料（有效在潮湿的环境中向外排除湿气）</li><li>天然，无溶剂，低过敏性</li><li>吸异味，优化室内空气质量</li><li>天然抗菌</li></ul><p><b>缺点：</b></p><ul><li>色卡比较有限</li><li>比较难控制其斑驳阴影的效果</li><li>为了达到预期效果估计要上好几层浆</li><li>清洗不方便，需要再次上浆。</li></ul><p>你宝宝觉得这样天然禅意的涂料应该在国内更加普及些吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;670&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da320ec015bf82bf5946d1e5d0518d2f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"344\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"344\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "环保牌粮油店", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95acc6c6c81795908f5a8845776ef6d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"393\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95acc6c6c81795908f5a8845776ef6d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;393&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"393\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95acc6c6c81795908f5a8845776ef6d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95acc6c6c81795908f5a8845776ef6d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>2019年刚开年，一家加拿大温哥华走在环保前沿的“零包装浪费”粮油店就进入大众视线, 名叫The Soap Dispensary。并被西方媒体预言到是未来零售业发展的热点。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2119bc189314218120862690df10d6cf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"473\" data-rawheight=\"642\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"473\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2119bc189314218120862690df10d6cf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;473&#39; height=&#39;642&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"473\" data-rawheight=\"642\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"473\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2119bc189314218120862690df10d6cf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2119bc189314218120862690df10d6cf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>店名翻译为“洗洁精补给店”会不会有点草率？但我设想发起人可能就是从一个晚上睡不着觉而胡思乱想的简单顾虑开始：你想想，光/洗洁精/洗手液/沐浴乳/洗护发露/洗衣液/柴米油盐醋/等等/每家每年会用掉几瓶？丢弃的塑料瓶或玻璃瓶会给地球造成多大的环保压力？如果我们可以一直使用同样的容器，能够减少多少的浪费？这个世界会变得多么美好...？（憧憬中）</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60237eae6b22d0d6017fcd1bcc7da262_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"977\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60237eae6b22d0d6017fcd1bcc7da262_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;977&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"977\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60237eae6b22d0d6017fcd1bcc7da262_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-60237eae6b22d0d6017fcd1bcc7da262_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>所以The Soap Dispensary主营产品的思路就是从<b>补给高频日常厨卫用品/食品</b>这个角度入手的，倡导大家循环使用容器，拿着自家瓶瓶罐罐来“续杯”。如果你是一个有着环保意识的潮人，他们还出售美美的玻璃罐。当然如果你比较实惠，可以去店里回收区自取一些免费的二手玻璃罐，重点是“不-浪-费”。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-555ee4b2f664fc7bbd8a09db3b334ac4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"977\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-555ee4b2f664fc7bbd8a09db3b334ac4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;977&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"977\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-555ee4b2f664fc7bbd8a09db3b334ac4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-555ee4b2f664fc7bbd8a09db3b334ac4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>对，就像这样打啤酒一样打油！还有背景彩色的瓶瓶罐罐，是香料？是花茶？家边上有这样的小店，是不是会令人想要开始善待自己，善待他人，善待地球那种过三好日子的冲动？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61dc4beba1d31cffc3bf2832a9946934_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1326\" data-rawheight=\"884\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1326\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61dc4beba1d31cffc3bf2832a9946934_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1326&#39; height=&#39;884&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1326\" data-rawheight=\"884\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1326\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61dc4beba1d31cffc3bf2832a9946934_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-61dc4beba1d31cffc3bf2832a9946934_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实，这样有环保意识的街角小店到如今被国际媒体报道，他们已经“潜伏”营业了近8年了。自2011年起，Linh Truoung 和 Stewart Lampe这对潮人夫妇开始贩卖一些环保日用品：比如手工香皂，木头/竹子手柄牙刷，无毒妇女卫生用品，散装洗洁精等。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-722afca081756d85f51420aa124578f4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-722afca081756d85f51420aa124578f4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;2199&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-722afca081756d85f51420aa124578f4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-722afca081756d85f51420aa124578f4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>8年来，小店生意红火到如今他们把业务范围拓展到食品类：散装干货，新鲜和速冻食品等。包装的问题不仅存在与日用品，食物也是高频消耗品。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-194ef48fb1a2b091350597e7eb6a488b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-194ef48fb1a2b091350597e7eb6a488b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;2199&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-194ef48fb1a2b091350597e7eb6a488b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-194ef48fb1a2b091350597e7eb6a488b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这样的健康的生活方式受到了当地居民的追捧。别看店面大而宽敞，一到周末就挤满了人。这种回归原始的零售方式在效率上肯定不如大规模生产和包装来得快捷，好多人在yelp上评价他们在称重时会比较耽误时间，有些还抱怨店员潮人态度多了些，亲和力就少了些。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-26a75d5718746010b2ce9a10b31a699b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"410\" data-rawheight=\"275\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"410\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;410&#39; height=&#39;275&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"410\" data-rawheight=\"275\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"410\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-26a75d5718746010b2ce9a10b31a699b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实，环保牌粮油店一直存在在国人的记忆中。上世纪80-90年代，每个小区里都有这样一家粮油店吧！作为80后的我还有小时候和妈妈一起去买粮油店买米的记忆。带着自备的米袋，套在粮店储米柜的出口处，营业员一声，准备好了吗？然后，“哗”的一声，米从大漏斗中一倾而下。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3319d75c315da4e122d323ccbac89def_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"333\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3319d75c315da4e122d323ccbac89def_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;500&#39; height=&#39;333&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"500\" data-rawheight=\"333\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"500\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3319d75c315da4e122d323ccbac89def_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3319d75c315da4e122d323ccbac89def_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>打食用油，酱油，醋什么的，也是得提着自家的油瓶，醋瓶子。当时怎么知道环保不环保，所有都从经济实惠角度出发。原来的“实惠牌”粮油店，现在已浪漫得化身为“环保牌”粮油店了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2302d73da42bbd29d08d187cc4de598b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2302d73da42bbd29d08d187cc4de598b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;2199&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2199\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2302d73da42bbd29d08d187cc4de598b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2302d73da42bbd29d08d187cc4de598b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实这么推崇环保是有其社会背景的，住在美国后我发现美国人的环保意识和欧洲相比还是差很多的：每次从超市出来，收营员就拼了命得给你的食物套上了好几层塑料袋，似乎这是一种礼遇。而欧洲人去超市几乎每个人都会自带购物袋。即便是国内，记得有一整子为了宣传环保，超市的塑料袋是要收费的。</p><p>我想这样“概念复古”的粮油店能回潮可能也是物质生活实在太丰厚，以至于大众目睹了太多的浪费了，而有环保意识的消费会令人更加身心愉悦。</p><p>期待这样的环保牌粮油店能够成为连锁。</p><p>从明天开始我要过三好生活。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;670&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-da320ec015bf82bf5946d1e5d0518d2f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"344\" data-rawheight=\"344\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"344\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "title": "中西合璧的田园生活是这样配方的", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f04f8c74bed0e3241b281ae881a1ab52_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f04f8c74bed0e3241b281ae881a1ab52_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f04f8c74bed0e3241b281ae881a1ab52_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f04f8c74bed0e3241b281ae881a1ab52_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>故事的女主是出生在日本的植物造型师Yasuyo Harvey，自从2004年留学伦敦后就顺利得留在了那里：嫁人，生子，还把家安在了郊外的一座1930年建造的老房子里，过起了宁静的田园生活，中西杂交的，就像她的5岁宝贝儿子Noah。对，跟刘烨的宝宝一个名。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a29feeb37feb6198045b38ef48d31bf9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"602\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a29feeb37feb6198045b38ef48d31bf9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;900&#39; height=&#39;602&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"900\" data-rawheight=\"602\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"900\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a29feeb37feb6198045b38ef48d31bf9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a29feeb37feb6198045b38ef48d31bf9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>怎么样？是不是可爱的想去咬一口。（左边的宝宝）</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4025527b53a8d36c1095463ddbbed4aa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"902\" data-rawheight=\"588\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"902\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4025527b53a8d36c1095463ddbbed4aa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;902&#39; height=&#39;588&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"902\" data-rawheight=\"588\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"902\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4025527b53a8d36c1095463ddbbed4aa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4025527b53a8d36c1095463ddbbed4aa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>伦敦郊外是这样的画风，同样，一个瘦小的日本女子穿上了英国粗壮轮廓的风衣和雨鞋。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a3526ffb9165e9728a56c5858fef9921_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"602\" data-rawheight=\"892\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"602\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a3526ffb9165e9728a56c5858fef9921_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;602&#39; height=&#39;892&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"602\" data-rawheight=\"892\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"602\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a3526ffb9165e9728a56c5858fef9921_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a3526ffb9165e9728a56c5858fef9921_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>没有特别大的来头，一个小女子在国外仅凭着对园艺和生活的热爱，现在的生活过得有滋有味。即使住在郊区，也时常有朋友拜访；虽是园艺师，但是家居装也非常可圈可点：这样高袜配真皮拖鞋拿出来就是街拍。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-87838fd4c843d03beb6ffe4e3bad17c7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1219\" data-rawheight=\"898\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1219\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-87838fd4c843d03beb6ffe4e3bad17c7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1219&#39; height=&#39;898&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1219\" data-rawheight=\"898\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1219\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-87838fd4c843d03beb6ffe4e3bad17c7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-87838fd4c843d03beb6ffe4e3bad17c7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>从开始在一家伦敦花店做帮工，然后再慢慢开始给派到伦敦工作的日本人开花艺课，她都过得默默无闻。直到有一年帮朋友当翻译一起去了巴黎时装周后，她碰上了英国著名设计师姐妹Faye 和 Erica Toogood，就被邀请去给她们的工作室做花艺造型。上面左边这幅就是她的作品。细心的你可以看出，Yasuyo的作品运用西方灌木植物，却做出了东方韵味的侘寂感。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-013bbacff9a479951024c56cc06b7c46_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-013bbacff9a479951024c56cc06b7c46_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;634&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-013bbacff9a479951024c56cc06b7c46_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-013bbacff9a479951024c56cc06b7c46_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>用心生活，每个人都是生活的艺术家。</b>看看这个富有生活情趣的园艺师是如何装饰/布置自己的家的吧！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4bba3f9f67a4091e85999fae7d404ca7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4bba3f9f67a4091e85999fae7d404ca7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4bba3f9f67a4091e85999fae7d404ca7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4bba3f9f67a4091e85999fae7d404ca7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>可能是延续了女主日本侘寂（wabi sabi）的灵魂吧，小夫妻两剥去墙纸后，发现石膏底墙呈现一种粗糙原质表面长时间使用后的损耗美感，于是就愉快的决定按原样保留墙体。</p><p>由于当地水泥材质价格会比较贵，地板采用了树脂材料，但他们承认树脂地板的确特别容易有刮痕。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e3ab77dc34f114d636b500f1c5c36891_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e3ab77dc34f114d636b500f1c5c36891_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;634&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e3ab77dc34f114d636b500f1c5c36891_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e3ab77dc34f114d636b500f1c5c36891_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>整个空间简单素雅，再配上一些老木头家具，以及工业元素的灯具。墙上，挂着的是园艺图册中的彩页。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-258afb0f60e7543805d742cbaf1407f0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-258afb0f60e7543805d742cbaf1407f0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-258afb0f60e7543805d742cbaf1407f0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-258afb0f60e7543805d742cbaf1407f0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>窗外，小夫妻两搞了一片方地，那是园艺材料库。Yasuyo说，最好的插花材料来自邻居家前院和小巷中。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c8c9501936233c6e5e5c972ed4d8bb5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"780\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c8c9501936233c6e5e5c972ed4d8bb5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;780&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"780\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c8c9501936233c6e5e5c972ed4d8bb5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8c8c9501936233c6e5e5c972ed4d8bb5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>说到插花，作为一个园艺师，家里怎能缺少一个插花点？按照园中植物春夏秋冬的变化和更替，Yasuyo应景应情的来插花。从她的ins账户中我发现除了灵感，作为一个严谨的日本人，她会研习不同的植物插花的可能性，以便之后的运用。</p><p>有时，邻居发现自家芍药长得极好（左上图作品），给她剪下几只，也是常有的事。插花也成为了情感交流的一个理由。右图中带有子的充满空间感的植物给插花的造型带去海绵般的质地。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3524b245f6053f53e96d980ba04b5742_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3524b245f6053f53e96d980ba04b5742_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3524b245f6053f53e96d980ba04b5742_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3524b245f6053f53e96d980ba04b5742_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>再来看看厨房，你就会发现，其实他们的装修并不豪华。然而有了花艺，即便是枯枝败叶也给陋室生出了无限气质。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-968d3b38b5885039f8bc2cd0499db8f7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"594\" data-rawheight=\"890\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"594\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-968d3b38b5885039f8bc2cd0499db8f7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;594&#39; height=&#39;890&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"594\" data-rawheight=\"890\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"594\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-968d3b38b5885039f8bc2cd0499db8f7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-968d3b38b5885039f8bc2cd0499db8f7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>家里最抢眼的就是这几张小木椅了吧。几件小古董和边上竖在墙边的枯枝败叶相得益彰。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2a57f88679091f02cebbd2ddad8b5341_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1067\" data-rawheight=\"1600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1067\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2a57f88679091f02cebbd2ddad8b5341_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1067&#39; height=&#39;1600&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1067\" data-rawheight=\"1600\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1067\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2a57f88679091f02cebbd2ddad8b5341_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2a57f88679091f02cebbd2ddad8b5341_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>同样，卧室也是木质家具，似乎很东方的元素却以西式家居的外形呈现。好一个东韵西境。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6aedd5b53be34f180ff96dd7dbc336c5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6aedd5b53be34f180ff96dd7dbc336c5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;634&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"634\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6aedd5b53be34f180ff96dd7dbc336c5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6aedd5b53be34f180ff96dd7dbc336c5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>屋子的一角摆设着干海藻和珊瑚。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f41b51b9a2ecdda4119a39edb8f83ec_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"1426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f41b51b9a2ecdda4119a39edb8f83ec_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;950&#39; height=&#39;1426&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"950\" data-rawheight=\"1426\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"950\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f41b51b9a2ecdda4119a39edb8f83ec_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-2f41b51b9a2ecdda4119a39edb8f83ec_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后来一张全家福。看看宝宝的头发是不是麻麻的发型+爸爸的发色？另外，粗针剑麻地毯在这样天然的环境中也是绝配。<br/>这样侘寂田园风格的家，这样一个以静生动的生活方式，正中你下怀吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "用黄铜正确点亮2019方式是这样的", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ed10b3630be0a614294465cf5d19a9ab_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ed10b3630be0a614294465cf5d19a9ab_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;750&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"750\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ed10b3630be0a614294465cf5d19a9ab_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ed10b3630be0a614294465cf5d19a9ab_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>黄铜，外表如金，却不如金子贵重，暗藏着奢华的气质，这几年非常受大众追捧。从色彩心理学角度看，<b>金色是财富和权利的象征，更深层次来看，金色使人认可自我价值，充满自信。</b>2019年开年，在家里稍稍运用金色的黄铜，可以召唤来年成功的能量。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>事实上，黄铜作为室内家装元素，已经流行了好一段时间了。以至于，随便翻开家装自家秀，就能看到黄铜闪闪发光的身影。有时候甚至是有些泛滥了，比如下图。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-64936ddaaf22708fdf5865129b252036_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1028\" data-rawheight=\"918\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1028\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-64936ddaaf22708fdf5865129b252036_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1028&#39; height=&#39;918&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1028\" data-rawheight=\"918\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1028\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-64936ddaaf22708fdf5865129b252036_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-64936ddaaf22708fdf5865129b252036_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>少量用黄铜点缀室内会给人一种高档豪华的感觉；但<b>如果大量使用，又不会驾驭，反而给人一种金色闪瞎眼的廉价感，使自信变成自负，让周围人产生抗拒心理</b>。黄铜虽好，可不要用力过猛哦。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7fab39217dcf23c14bcf2b3d34d71a54_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1056\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7fab39217dcf23c14bcf2b3d34d71a54_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;1056&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1056\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7fab39217dcf23c14bcf2b3d34d71a54_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7fab39217dcf23c14bcf2b3d34d71a54_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>给完反面例子后，再来看看一个正面例子。这两个室内的配色，材质上其实非常相似，但是后者看起来就和谐许多。点缀期间的金色黄铜被足够多的深色元素所中和，所以并未有张扬之嫌。 <b>一个治愈而平衡的住宅空间里，请用合适的比例来用黄铜元素点缀空间。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-066a8a7a6a72a4017560d09737877016_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1233\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1233\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-066a8a7a6a72a4017560d09737877016_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1233&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1233\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1233\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-066a8a7a6a72a4017560d09737877016_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-066a8a7a6a72a4017560d09737877016_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>另外，由于<b>表面的不同处理</b>，黄铜会表现出不同的性格，召唤不同的能量。抛了光的黄铜给人一种皇宫大殿般的华丽感。在这样但空间里呆的时间久了，人容易感觉浮躁不安，不利于静心养神，最不适宜运用在卧室里；哑光的黄铜好像一个洗去铅华的人，通过它，好像能看到岁月的沉淀，更具魅力。</p><p>事实上，国外已经有家装媒体在大胆预测<b>“无黄铜不欢的室内设计”</b>将会在2019年变得过时，有些甚至开始拥抱深褐色的铜质五金件。看来是整个国际社会都在从一个过分高调张扬的养成性格中，过渡到内敛踏实的作风去。</p><p>那么，如何才是高段位使用黄铜的方法，去潜移默化一个<b>自信又低调</b>的人格呢？<br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f27a611a9daf27fff052f7449fa34148_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f27a611a9daf27fff052f7449fa34148_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f27a611a9daf27fff052f7449fa34148_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f27a611a9daf27fff052f7449fa34148_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da0c1405726829fb33482c2806137b81_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"667\" data-rawheight=\"446\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"667\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da0c1405726829fb33482c2806137b81_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;667&#39; height=&#39;446&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"667\" data-rawheight=\"446\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"667\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da0c1405726829fb33482c2806137b81_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-da0c1405726829fb33482c2806137b81_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>喜欢极简空间的宝宝们，可以用一个黄铜的吊灯，或是浴室五金点亮黑白灰色调的空间。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2bf6c5b69c94e87186faf999ed1a9679_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"433\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2bf6c5b69c94e87186faf999ed1a9679_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;650&#39; height=&#39;433&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"650\" data-rawheight=\"433\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"650\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2bf6c5b69c94e87186faf999ed1a9679_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2bf6c5b69c94e87186faf999ed1a9679_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>断舍离的目的不是出世，而是为了整理自我价值，然后更好的轻装上路。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7615d98ba93de65dc1b2f2e55a6d3fa7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7615d98ba93de65dc1b2f2e55a6d3fa7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7615d98ba93de65dc1b2f2e55a6d3fa7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-7615d98ba93de65dc1b2f2e55a6d3fa7_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb16aa75ac70123f7dc0e968ec424f54_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1742\" data-rawheight=\"1500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1742\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb16aa75ac70123f7dc0e968ec424f54_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1742&#39; height=&#39;1500&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1742\" data-rawheight=\"1500\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1742\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb16aa75ac70123f7dc0e968ec424f54_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb16aa75ac70123f7dc0e968ec424f54_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>为什么说黄铜复古？除去近代art deco和中古风格的灯饰里很多运用黄铜元素，远的还能想到欧洲皇宫里的襄金画框（虽然里头是木头芯子的，但是外观看起来和黄铜没什么两样），古堡里的黄铜水晶大吊灯，还有黄铜烛台。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3a2d2a406dcb3e41580a558a8c5e5134_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"704\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3a2d2a406dcb3e41580a558a8c5e5134_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;704&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"704\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3a2d2a406dcb3e41580a558a8c5e5134_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3a2d2a406dcb3e41580a558a8c5e5134_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>由于这种历史记忆，<u>形态简洁的黄铜灯具</u>和<u>欧式范儿的护墙板</u>有种与生俱来的夫妻相。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fec2fdd327a403c6bba3c46c003a54b1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1160\" data-rawheight=\"1534\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1160\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fec2fdd327a403c6bba3c46c003a54b1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1160&#39; height=&#39;1534&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1160\" data-rawheight=\"1534\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1160\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fec2fdd327a403c6bba3c46c003a54b1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fec2fdd327a403c6bba3c46c003a54b1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f22ad54deb9ffc71828871ce39438884_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f22ad54deb9ffc71828871ce39438884_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f22ad54deb9ffc71828871ce39438884_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f22ad54deb9ffc71828871ce39438884_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e2e6e77c608c21eb6fdbbe4a799c2942_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1301\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1301\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e2e6e77c608c21eb6fdbbe4a799c2942_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1301&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1301\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1301\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e2e6e77c608c21eb6fdbbe4a799c2942_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e2e6e77c608c21eb6fdbbe4a799c2942_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>黄铜不仅是属于西方历史记忆的，在布满岁月感的老木箱子上，黄铜是雕花锁片；文房四宝丛中，黄铜好像是金刚护法。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-570a41b19fe815bd47fb23c05f96f60e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"760\" data-rawheight=\"626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"760\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-570a41b19fe815bd47fb23c05f96f60e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;760&#39; height=&#39;626&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"760\" data-rawheight=\"626\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"760\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-570a41b19fe815bd47fb23c05f96f60e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-570a41b19fe815bd47fb23c05f96f60e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>木头和黄铜，一个柔韧随和，一个坚硬锋芒；深色的木头和亮色的黄铜，一个老成内敛，一个耀眼夺目。似乎也是绝配。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-acf4b595fc0c7ad12d66324678bbad7c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-acf4b595fc0c7ad12d66324678bbad7c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-acf4b595fc0c7ad12d66324678bbad7c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-acf4b595fc0c7ad12d66324678bbad7c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这样的组合可以是老木柜配上黄铜灯饰。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7e1451c50647cc29e8cbf2463ec57178_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"813\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7e1451c50647cc29e8cbf2463ec57178_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;813&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"813\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7e1451c50647cc29e8cbf2463ec57178_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7e1451c50647cc29e8cbf2463ec57178_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>可以是深色的老木地板配上黄铜灯饰。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-58450d3d3dd5101b1f53dbbb98c9c6f1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"848\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-58450d3d3dd5101b1f53dbbb98c9c6f1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;848&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"848\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-58450d3d3dd5101b1f53dbbb98c9c6f1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-58450d3d3dd5101b1f53dbbb98c9c6f1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>还有这样的简洁现代空间里的现代木质家具和黄铜搭配也可以参考。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4025b223cb29476e534204e0fe3a8e37_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4025b223cb29476e534204e0fe3a8e37_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4025b223cb29476e534204e0fe3a8e37_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4025b223cb29476e534204e0fe3a8e37_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cd6044b7e31f7ac025702f7c73d03e00_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2217\" data-rawheight=\"1526\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2217\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cd6044b7e31f7ac025702f7c73d03e00_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2217&#39; height=&#39;1526&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2217\" data-rawheight=\"1526\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2217\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cd6044b7e31f7ac025702f7c73d03e00_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cd6044b7e31f7ac025702f7c73d03e00_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果用一个朴素的材质搭配高贵的黄铜，营造出的空间会是什么调调的呢？上图中墙面的涂料是一种石灰质地的涂料（lime wash），虽然看起来非常低调，但是这是一种比较高档的涂料。配上黄铜材质的灯具，勾出空间潜在的高档气质。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9266ef3227ba3328f906756b7e0279ab_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"957\" data-rawheight=\"604\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"957\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9266ef3227ba3328f906756b7e0279ab_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;957&#39; height=&#39;604&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"957\" data-rawheight=\"604\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"957\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9266ef3227ba3328f906756b7e0279ab_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9266ef3227ba3328f906756b7e0279ab_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>在像水泥或砖块内墙的毛坯房这样朴素粗燥的环境中，黄铜元素加强了其工业感，土土的室内一下就时髦起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-39d5bee22e023872a9e8906ae06088ea_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"668\" data-rawheight=\"959\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"668\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-39d5bee22e023872a9e8906ae06088ea_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;668&#39; height=&#39;959&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"668\" data-rawheight=\"959\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"668\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-39d5bee22e023872a9e8906ae06088ea_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-39d5bee22e023872a9e8906ae06088ea_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d13d7b9060b53e1a64a9b8428d8565ff_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d13d7b9060b53e1a64a9b8428d8565ff_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;3002&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"3002\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"3002\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d13d7b9060b53e1a64a9b8428d8565ff_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-d13d7b9060b53e1a64a9b8428d8565ff_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fa0ecb33aa7c2174444cdfede81f231f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1149\" data-rawheight=\"733\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1149\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fa0ecb33aa7c2174444cdfede81f231f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1149&#39; height=&#39;733&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1149\" data-rawheight=\"733\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1149\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fa0ecb33aa7c2174444cdfede81f231f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fa0ecb33aa7c2174444cdfede81f231f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>最后来说说颜色搭配。黄铜和深绿色似乎是不会错的搭配，在自家秀的图片里上镜率超高。但是我想说还有很多出彩的搭配色系。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-22f98dd4d891aa6eaa2315e737e205ed_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"523\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"523\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-22f98dd4d891aa6eaa2315e737e205ed_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;523&#39; height=&#39;523&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"523\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"523\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-22f98dd4d891aa6eaa2315e737e205ed_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-22f98dd4d891aa6eaa2315e737e205ed_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb8f4a205304b1c49da4f27f3c0c1964_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"737\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-cb8f4a205304b1c49da4f27f3c0c1964_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;627&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"627\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-888ff7ec9c7e92ef054f5f14d0e848d8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-888ff7ec9c7e92ef054f5f14d0e848d8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>设计段位高的你可以挑战华丽的色彩配置。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-917a4a58625d517ee282799a62f99fbb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1027\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1027\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-917a4a58625d517ee282799a62f99fbb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1027&#39; height=&#39;676&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1027\" data-rawheight=\"676\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1027\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-917a4a58625d517ee282799a62f99fbb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-917a4a58625d517ee282799a62f99fbb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>无论是什么色系，搭配黄铜时要注意用<b>反差色</b>来凸显黄铜的亮感。</p><p>上面在网上找出的两张图中，同样都是黄铜茶几，明显右边这张中黄铜的使用比左边这张要精彩的多了。分析一下原因，👆左图中地板的颜色和黄铜同色系；👆右图中地板颜色黑漆色，即使地板也是光面，但是光一个黑色就给黄铜形成了绝对的对比。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-843090ef2b1ec5ddabfd03a0bbbe043c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1244\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1244\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-843090ef2b1ec5ddabfd03a0bbbe043c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1244&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1244\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1244\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-843090ef2b1ec5ddabfd03a0bbbe043c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-843090ef2b1ec5ddabfd03a0bbbe043c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>当然，黄铜搭配<b>同色系</b>，不同材质的元素也很有调和感，比如左上图。右上图颜色比较杂，既没有对比也不调和，黄铜存在感非常差。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
