width=&#39;1847&#39; height=&#39;1507&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1847\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1847\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8b1569eef6e715a812ec6332671f3803_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-8b1569eef6e715a812ec6332671f3803_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>而纽约的房子基本都是这样一面墙上有两个窗子，而窗户都是从下向上推开的。偶尔看到国内一些特别的户型也会有一面墙上并排两扇窗。窗户多了，视觉上也是有一种对称的节奏美感，叠加在窗户上的窗帘也一样。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4c34f114b16d67159b1780344b5d7aaf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1163\" data-rawheight=\"583\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1163\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4c34f114b16d67159b1780344b5d7aaf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1163&#39; height=&#39;583&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1163\" data-rawheight=\"583\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1163\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4c34f114b16d67159b1780344b5d7aaf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4c34f114b16d67159b1780344b5d7aaf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>看看是不是？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1fe69441602128e5dcd9758589bec450_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"1456\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1fe69441602128e5dcd9758589bec450_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;1456&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"1456\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1fe69441602128e5dcd9758589bec450_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-1fe69441602128e5dcd9758589bec450_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>不管是单窗还是双窗，窗帘安装的原则都差不多：就是要看起来亭亭玉立才比较美。<b>所以一般情况下，设计师们都喜欢把窗帘架到房顶这里，再慢慢垂下来。</b>这样，房间也看起来似乎高了许多。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-edfba861cb7d239e424468303e1b9b2d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"628\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-edfba861cb7d239e424468303e1b9b2d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1200&#39; height=&#39;628&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"628\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-edfba861cb7d239e424468303e1b9b2d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-edfba861cb7d239e424468303e1b9b2d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>在选择窗帘的时候要注意挂钩的类型，会决定推拉窗帘的难易，以及窗帘悬挂时看起来是否整齐。都是这些细节中见设计的高低，所以不能不注意。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-80c87dcbbf6ee51a27fa982ca8bf6991_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1103\" data-rawheight=\"825\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1103\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-80c87dcbbf6ee51a27fa982ca8bf6991_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1103&#39; height=&#39;825&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1103\" data-rawheight=\"825\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1103\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-80c87dcbbf6ee51a27fa982ca8bf6991_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-80c87dcbbf6ee51a27fa982ca8bf6991_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>有转角的窗帘杆使得窗帘立体得把窗户包围起来，市面上不是特别常见，但其实宜家就有买这样但转角窗帘杆，就看你有没有这样的小心机了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c8fde81424931cf2ca189f2c26cac70_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>整面墙窗/落地移门窗<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69ef6cee2dab71f4d841497bc7a5d345_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1842\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1842\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69ef6cee2dab71f4d841497bc7a5d345_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1842&#39; height=&#39;1507&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1842\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1842\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69ef6cee2dab71f4d841497bc7a5d345_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-69ef6cee2dab71f4d841497bc7a5d345_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>客厅或卧室和阳台之间的落地窗也是国内户型中比较常见的窗户了。如果是客厅，房顶上一般都会做吊顶，所以这里需要注意的就是吊顶和窗帘的关系。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5d21c473f816b7ec0ea2e128814475e6_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5d21c473f816b7ec0ea2e128814475e6_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;461&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5d21c473f816b7ec0ea2e128814475e6_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5d21c473f816b7ec0ea2e128814475e6_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>比如这幅图中乍眼一看好像比较华丽，但却总觉得好像有些地方不协调。仔细一看这个窗帘的帘罩再加上那么深的吊顶把立面分成了三大块，视觉上缩短了层高，让我不得不吐槽。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f403121c4a501e6f165b0dae97168b64_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"732\" data-rawheight=\"424\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"732\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f403121c4a501e6f165b0dae97168b64_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;732&#39; height=&#39;424&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"732\" data-rawheight=\"424\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"732\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f403121c4a501e6f165b0dae97168b64_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f403121c4a501e6f165b0dae97168b64_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这幅图和上面的例子有同样的问题。另外，还用上了这样的硬窗帘罩（cornice），让空间显得局促拥挤，简直辣人眼。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6a63ce27527b271c0655067bbc2188d8_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6a63ce27527b271c0655067bbc2188d8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;376&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6a63ce27527b271c0655067bbc2188d8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-6a63ce27527b271c0655067bbc2188d8_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>来看看些正面的例子吧！这个平吊顶和周围墙体间留了些距离，把窗帘头隐藏在缝隙中。没有过多的装饰，反而特别符合本来空间就不大的现代城市住宅。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cebfda0e67aa6e140359a0123f718bef_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1152\" data-rawheight=\"468\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1152\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cebfda0e67aa6e140359a0123f718bef_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1152&#39; height=&#39;468&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1152\" data-rawheight=\"468\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1152\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cebfda0e67aa6e140359a0123f718bef_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-cebfda0e67aa6e140359a0123f718bef_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这个例子在吊顶上没有浪费空间，只是做了薄薄的一圈石膏板：留出足够的层高，巧妙的遮挡了窗帘，还勾勒了屋顶的边缘。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8f106d6e26be36b71a5903e93ad06f72_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1107\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1107\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8f106d6e26be36b71a5903e93ad06f72_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1107&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1107\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1107\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8f106d6e26be36b71a5903e93ad06f72_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8f106d6e26be36b71a5903e93ad06f72_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实，这种能够嵌入房顶的窗帘轨道才是我的最爱：简约大方，没有任何矫饰。顺便一提，窗帘的转角设计柔化了四四方方的房间角落。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-787b2844e24bcd6f30d437f7ce83d6d5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1041\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-787b2844e24bcd6f30d437f7ce83d6d5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;1041&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"1041\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-787b2844e24bcd6f30d437f7ce83d6d5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-787b2844e24bcd6f30d437f7ce83d6d5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这个卧室好美，除了那条惊艳的咸菜绿的窗帘和卧室其他颜色的搭配以外，大家有没有注意到<b>窗帘的边缘也用上了微微的转角，柔化了房间的棱角，给人一种房间是圆角的错觉？</b></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3156d83871ad8ed56bd72813ea11a94d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>飘窗<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b3fcc120ae622b476dec27fa94b6b129_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"918\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b3fcc120ae622b476dec27fa94b6b129_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;918&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"918\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b3fcc120ae622b476dec27fa94b6b129_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b3fcc120ae622b476dec27fa94b6b129_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>被墙体或者收纳柜包围的飘窗到底应该把窗帘挂在飘窗内还是外面呢？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c903c51844d51c442e6413f96269966_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"710\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c903c51844d51c442e6413f96269966_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;710&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"710\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c903c51844d51c442e6413f96269966_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c903c51844d51c442e6413f96269966_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这个在网上找来的例子就比较诡异。看起来好像是飘窗被箱体包围着，但是这个不对称的“箱体”其实是窗帘箱。视觉上这面墙被切割成三段式，让本来就不大的空间显得更加低矮和拥挤。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-83aa6d5c434cd734f42caf59c419a2d4_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1056\" data-rawheight=\"857\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1056\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-83aa6d5c434cd734f42caf59c419a2d4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1056&#39; height=&#39;857&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1056\" data-rawheight=\"857\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1056\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-83aa6d5c434cd734f42caf59c419a2d4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-83aa6d5c434cd734f42caf59c419a2d4_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果上面的例子把窗帘挂在飘窗外面是不是感觉空间更加清爽？被窗户切开的墙体在窗帘的掩饰下又合成一体。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f40c18350d794da4dca4601a19745ec1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"575\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f40c18350d794da4dca4601a19745ec1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;575&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"575\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f40c18350d794da4dca4601a19745ec1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f40c18350d794da4dca4601a19745ec1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>这种把窗帘挂在刚好飘窗里面的外围，和抱枕一起慵懒得散落在窗边，是不是让用有公主梦的你心里痒痒的？</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712781820b20452292ff87d455bc6eaa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1847\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1847\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712781820b20452292ff87d455bc6eaa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1847&#39; height=&#39;1507&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1847\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1847\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712781820b20452292ff87d455bc6eaa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-712781820b20452292ff87d455bc6eaa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>还有一种飘窗周围没有柜体的包围，看起来比较开阔，比较适合下面这样的窗帘安装。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-07ee8a75ca45d04dab33d80aa1ce768e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"697\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-07ee8a75ca45d04dab33d80aa1ce768e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;697&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"697\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-07ee8a75ca45d04dab33d80aa1ce768e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-07ee8a75ca45d04dab33d80aa1ce768e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-60a3b8cb88f639aeef2a1e5eefa85534_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>角落窗<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c60a654274e79a9606b85edfc56d54cc_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1842\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1842\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c60a654274e79a9606b85edfc56d54cc_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1842&#39; height=&#39;1507&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1842\" data-rawheight=\"1507\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1842\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c60a654274e79a9606b85edfc56d54cc_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c60a654274e79a9606b85edfc56d54cc_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>说实话，我非常惊讶窗户竟然还有这样鸡贼的存在。另外，两边开窗竟然大小不一样！比如下图。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-196d865cd26c0bdb4344ae21cfb62703_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-196d865cd26c0bdb4344ae21cfb62703_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;497&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"497\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-196d865cd26c0bdb4344ae21cfb62703_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-196d865cd26c0bdb4344ae21cfb62703_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如何改进这样的建筑审美缺陷？首先可以去掉这个肉麻的窗帘罩。然后呢，既然窗帘是房间的掩饰，可以运用窗帘来掩饰两个窗户不均的大小，来使视觉上达到平衡。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-397dbfbf0dda290b4b1dfc7f8335da46_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-397dbfbf0dda290b4b1dfc7f8335da46_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-397dbfbf0dda290b4b1dfc7f8335da46_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-397dbfbf0dda290b4b1dfc7f8335da46_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>我们来看一下优秀案例中窗帘罩（cornice）的运用方式。就如上图所示：</p><p>1. 窗帘罩不适合较长的窗户，而是窄而高的单窗，这样才亭亭玉立。</p><p>2. 窗帘罩源于贵族的室内装饰，如果做工上/质量上不到位，反而显得廉价。</p><p>3. 窗帘罩搭配双层窗帘，比较合适的是一层运用卷帘/百叶帘，另一层运用布艺窗帘。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b4b3f676131f418ccf43d26f28799e67_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1040\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b4b3f676131f418ccf43d26f28799e67_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1040&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1040\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b4b3f676131f418ccf43d26f28799e67_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b4b3f676131f418ccf43d26f28799e67_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实不用贵族的窗帘罩，简约大方的单层布艺窗帘对于转角窗户也足够了。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c9b95e4900af67be67e20f1dd9a8f10_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"879\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c9b95e4900af67be67e20f1dd9a8f10_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;879&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"879\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c9b95e4900af67be67e20f1dd9a8f10_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0c9b95e4900af67be67e20f1dd9a8f10_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果你觉得浪漫的布艺窗帘不是你的菜，那么卷帘则非常的干净利索。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5a8d06fd7ab07317390444d367ec5a7f_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5a8d06fd7ab07317390444d367ec5a7f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;4096&#39; height=&#39;288&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"4096\" data-rawheight=\"288\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"4096\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5a8d06fd7ab07317390444d367ec5a7f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5a8d06fd7ab07317390444d367ec5a7f_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>窗帘神奇的其他用途<br/></p><p>窗帘不仅仅是遮挡窗户用的，还有分割空间，遮挡视线，柔化棱角，增加室内舒适/华丽程度等作用。如果想高级的运用窗帘，打起精神来吧，下面都是自己总结的干货放送。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa1d802dfc2d9c6dec713031703279d9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa1d802dfc2d9c6dec713031703279d9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;705&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"705\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa1d802dfc2d9c6dec713031703279d9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa1d802dfc2d9c6dec713031703279d9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>对于这样比较方正的空间，设计师为了<b>柔化墙角</b>，安上了窗帘，同时也成为了书柜的滑门。柔软的窗帘+温润的木柜，室内材质丰富起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-48d8560357bad179224379536f48ed53_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1176\" data-rawheight=\"910\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1176\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-48d8560357bad179224379536f48ed53_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1176&#39; height=&#39;910&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1176\" data-rawheight=\"910\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1176\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-48d8560357bad179224379536f48ed53_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-48d8560357bad179224379536f48ed53_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>单副窗帘不成气候，多幅才能形成一个系统，互相呼应。如果你拥有一个比较开阔的卧室，何不用<b>窗帘包围床铺</b>，形成一个屋中屋？一来聚气，保证睡眠质量；二来也是很好的装饰，空旷的卧室一下变得温馨起来。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-189e7c8f2adb2e92895fd3cb7b494503_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"604\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"604\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-189e7c8f2adb2e92895fd3cb7b494503_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;604&#39; height=&#39;800&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"604\" data-rawheight=\"800\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"604\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-189e7c8f2adb2e92895fd3cb7b494503_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-189e7c8f2adb2e92895fd3cb7b494503_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>窗帘还能用来切割空间，优化一些奇葩户型。比如没有玄关的客厅，或是形状过于长方的客厅等等。<b>用窗帘作为分割，隔而不破空间，而且还可开可合，很是灵活。</b>上图中在工业感极强的空旷室内选用半透明而材质柔软的窗帘，有种温润浪漫的感觉。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-39b8ab2f3070403fa91eeb6f96f48e43_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-39b8ab2f3070403fa91eeb6f96f48e43_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-39b8ab2f3070403fa91eeb6f96f48e43_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-39b8ab2f3070403fa91eeb6f96f48e43_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>窗帘还可以当门来用：这样挽起可以改变死板的四方门洞线条，室内空间一下腰身变成了温暖的家。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522ca64517296559204942e046d0f483_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"754\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522ca64517296559204942e046d0f483_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;754&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"754\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522ca64517296559204942e046d0f483_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-522ca64517296559204942e046d0f483_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>单边挽起也有其独特慵懒的味道和文艺的腔调。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>最后，回到我老板对于Hell&#39;s Kitchen那户人家窗帘的处理的小秘密：配合屋内黄绿蓝色调，他在窗帘的内侧缝上了一条黄绿色的边，宜家买的窗帘一下就变成了订制窗帘，逼格上升好几个百分点。下一期我们就来讲讲如果选购不同材质和纹样的窗帘布艺，千万不要错过哦。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//weixin.qq.com/r/DS6-pxvEmkblrV-E93sf\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">http://</span><span class=\"visible\">weixin.qq.com/r/DS6-pxv</span><span class=\"invisible\">EmkblrV-E93sf</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a> (二维码自动识别)</p><p></p><p></p>",

            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e474143d13f5c7b19d51c9b92287fc20_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1191\" data-rawheight=\"785\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1191\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-e474143d13f5c7b19d51c9b92287fc20_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;200&#39; height=&#39;200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"200\" data-rawheight=\"200\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"200\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-92772481721feab5a496558314f22094_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>两天夜不能寐后，他突然接到一通电话，电话对面听起来是一个办事果断，声音强劲有力的帅哥（知道是帅哥因为他后来很积极得给我看了人家得照片）：“Peter, 我愿意免费借你我们家的地毯，看中什么都可以随便挑。” 然后老板大人就变成下面的这个德行：“那个朋友开得是一个古董家具店，好多拍电影的都去他们家租家具哦。”另外，他还津津乐道地和我说，这个古董店老板曾经和他的前男友拍拖过。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>“That’s gay connection, girl! ”</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-70f218ec933fd406d401a92e8bdf12ec_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"200\" data-rawheight=\"200\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"200\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;200&#39; height=&#39;200&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"200\" data-rawheight=\"200\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"200\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-70f218ec933fd406d401a92e8bdf12ec_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>我想了半天没想明白，为了一个地毯有必要扯出那么复杂的关系吗？</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4f441b06bb5e825dd5eb18b4e92af3e0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4f441b06bb5e825dd5eb18b4e92af3e0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4f441b06bb5e825dd5eb18b4e92af3e0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4f441b06bb5e825dd5eb18b4e92af3e0_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-783e8616960e14d3256814729bfc90c3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1173\" data-rawheight=\"760\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1173\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-783e8616960e14d3256814729bfc90c3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1173&#39; height=&#39;760&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1173\" data-rawheight=\"760\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1173\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-783e8616960e14d3256814729bfc90c3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-783e8616960e14d3256814729bfc90c3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一块地毯可以把两个gay连接起来，也可以把在室内行动的人和和地面连接起来。在室内人们一般在休憩区用餐区等长时间驻足的区域铺上地毯，同时地毯也给人休憩区域大小,甚至休憩时间的<b>心里暗示</b>。比如上图，用的地毯大小不同，给人一种休憩空间，甚至时间上的设定。👈的沙发区是不是感觉是为了小等片刻而准备的，而👉的沙发区在那里可以坐下便不起来了？<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ceb4ddf71611c80704e40b8f4c2e0f5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ceb4ddf71611c80704e40b8f4c2e0f5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ceb4ddf71611c80704e40b8f4c2e0f5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ceb4ddf71611c80704e40b8f4c2e0f5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>地毯可以让人驻足，也可以让人动起来。比如👆走道上的地毯则给人一种行动方向的暗示。这里本小编想到了奥斯卡红毯。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-44294bcd1e5cdc4383ce47af688de59d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-44294bcd1e5cdc4383ce47af688de59d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;846&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"846\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-44294bcd1e5cdc4383ce47af688de59d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-44294bcd1e5cdc4383ce47af688de59d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>其实，本小编更喜欢把地毯想成地板的衣服，光溜溜冷冰冰的地面上突然出现一块地毯，就好像沙漠里的绿洲一样，让空间一下子温馨起来。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c2d7dd374d7eddf0532f09fff09cbd25_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c2d7dd374d7eddf0532f09fff09cbd25_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c2d7dd374d7eddf0532f09fff09cbd25_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c2d7dd374d7eddf0532f09fff09cbd25_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e60fc60a66a954f56637c0ee34dd4b5d_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"739\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"739\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e60fc60a66a954f56637c0ee34dd4b5d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;739&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"739\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"739\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e60fc60a66a954f56637c0ee34dd4b5d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-e60fc60a66a954f56637c0ee34dd4b5d_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>看看市面上的各种地毯，有些是<b>化纤材质</b>的，有的是<b>羊毛材质</b>的，对于 Peter 这样自诩Snob的小gay来说，他只喜欢<b>丝绸材质</b>的地毯。看到这里不要惊慌，丝绸地毯不是你的丝绸睡衣的布料躺在地上就成了一块地毯。事实上，无论是什么材质，如果你不翻牌看成分，看起来都差不多，只是丝绸地毯看起来表面上闪着一层暗暗的光，低调又奢华。化纤地毯则可以模仿天然纤维地毯的外形，想想衣物其实就很好理解。<b>市面上的地毯大多是多种材质混纺，为了达到美观上，使用上以及价格方面的平衡点。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2293c0dce2bd884ffe4c2cef87e1ac23_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1300\" data-rawheight=\"792\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1300\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2293c0dce2bd884ffe4c2cef87e1ac23_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1300&#39; height=&#39;792&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1300\" data-rawheight=\"792\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1300\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2293c0dce2bd884ffe4c2cef87e1ac23_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2293c0dce2bd884ffe4c2cef87e1ac23_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 丝绸材质地毯</p><p>按现代人的常识，化纤的东西除了不环保以外，价格低廉，花样多，还耐用。其实，像<b>羊毛这样的天然纤维制成的地毯的不像想象中的那么娇贵。</b>羊毛地毯防水（但不保证仿红酒染色）还防火，另外一条优质羊毛地毯能够用50年以上呢！而“万能的化纤”地毯一般使用3-5年后，表面就会变脆而折断。虽然在防污渍方面比羊毛材质的地毯表现更加出色，但是却非常易燃（因为是石油制品）。丝绸材质的地毯则更娇贵些。各位宝宝们按自己喜好和需要各自对号选购。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c124a1f04fa7367b3377819563216d44_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"703\" data-rawheight=\"460\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"703\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c124a1f04fa7367b3377819563216d44_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;703&#39; height=&#39;460&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"703\" data-rawheight=\"460\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"703\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c124a1f04fa7367b3377819563216d44_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c124a1f04fa7367b3377819563216d44_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>另外，地毯的<b>毛长</b>也很有讲究。平织短毛最适合那些经常走动的区域；毛越长的地毯脚感越舒服，也越难打理，脏东西容易藏着厚厚的毛里。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3a529b218d93f2168aafa20fdd0f42b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"698\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3a529b218d93f2168aafa20fdd0f42b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;698&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"698\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3a529b218d93f2168aafa20fdd0f42b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c3a529b218d93f2168aafa20fdd0f42b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>长毛地毯娇贵，一般人大概不敢用，但用得好能给人一种奢华和好莱坞般的光彩，比较适合卧室等需要拖鞋的私密区域。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95cf70c20af35b44ebdaa531052fce5c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1136\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95cf70c20af35b44ebdaa531052fce5c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1136&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1136\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95cf70c20af35b44ebdaa531052fce5c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-95cf70c20af35b44ebdaa531052fce5c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>还有一种地毯是由各种<b>麻草类天然纤维</b>制成的。虽然给人一种朴素自然的感觉，但是脚感却很差，不适合赤脚踩在上面。由于不怕光照，麻草地毯比较适合和室外连接紧密的区域：比如阳台，也适合乡村风格的室内。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c6488a81112d25c3ee86c632f0047708_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c6488a81112d25c3ee86c632f0047708_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;376&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"376\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c6488a81112d25c3ee86c632f0047708_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c6488a81112d25c3ee86c632f0047708_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9f525a21a034ff55f4f8f527b371d1a3_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9f525a21a034ff55f4f8f527b371d1a3_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9f525a21a034ff55f4f8f527b371d1a3_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9f525a21a034ff55f4f8f527b371d1a3_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>一般搭配地毯的时候宝宝们可以参照家具的风格，如果是布艺沙发的话，看布艺的颜色和材质， 地板的颜色和纹样等等。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-572d20729330e19d341c2e14c9afcdaf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"510\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;510&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"510\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-572d20729330e19d341c2e14c9afcdaf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>地毯和抱枕的纹样可以搭配起来。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1f709dc23ed16eabfc7a632fe5da934b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1f709dc23ed16eabfc7a632fe5da934b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;564&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"564\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1f709dc23ed16eabfc7a632fe5da934b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-1f709dc23ed16eabfc7a632fe5da934b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>地毯和家具的风格可以非常搭配。天然麻草材质的地毯和深棕色的木质家具是绝配。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd0cfd624852b708f68479da68a87d0a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"678\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd0cfd624852b708f68479da68a87d0a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;678&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"678\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd0cfd624852b708f68479da68a87d0a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd0cfd624852b708f68479da68a87d0a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果嫌地板颜色太深，那么一块颜色鲜艳的地毯可以让整个空间欢快起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6cfa8c1102e52d00e2f2ca9dcb4628a5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6cfa8c1102e52d00e2f2ca9dcb4628a5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;564&#39; height=&#39;752&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"564\" data-rawheight=\"752\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"564\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6cfa8c1102e52d00e2f2ca9dcb4628a5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6cfa8c1102e52d00e2f2ca9dcb4628a5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>周五收工之前，Peter 和我透露了一个秘密，就是他会在已有的地毯上再加一张地毯：“这叫叠加，这样的话整个空间看起来会更大些。另外，两块地毯叠在一起就好像是你里外两件衣服的搭配，搭配得好了能透露满满的小心机。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>下周五就要给装修好的Hell&#39;s Kitchen项目拍照了，估计Peter 现在还在加班呢！各位宝宝们如果想看到最终呈现的作品，别忘了积极关注治愈家公众号哦！</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;             "userName": "治愈家杂志", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/d97614d3497ec610467aec3d7ae89f53", 
            "upvote": 2, 
            "title": "为什么《广告狂人》的中古风设计还没死？", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-94fc247e2dd765e407ef7f155a4f23d7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1048\" data-rawheight=\"947\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1048\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-94fc247e2dd765e407ef7f155a4f23d7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1048&#39; height=&#39;947&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1048\" data-rawheight=\"947\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1048\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-94fc247e2dd765e407ef7f155a4f23d7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-94fc247e2dd765e407ef7f155a4f23d7_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△  今年网上有关当今设计趋势的将会走向肥胖线条的文章，是对中古风格相对纤细形体的一种反叛。</p><p>已经有阵子有人大胆预测“中古风”（Mid century modern）已死，各种新潮流即将称霸江湖的消息被本小编亲身经验果断推翻。本小编在纽约某室内设计工作室上班的第一个项目就是翻新一套高端中古风格的私人住宅。对“中古风”这个风格不熟悉的宝宝们，请自动查找脑海里《广告狂人》的剧照。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04525db8fc7a1e935173dc8587f035ad_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"387\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04525db8fc7a1e935173dc8587f035ad_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;550&#39; height=&#39;387&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"550\" data-rawheight=\"387\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"550\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04525db8fc7a1e935173dc8587f035ad_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-04525db8fc7a1e935173dc8587f035ad_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>不仅是阿姨叔叔的家里，美国的90，00后都是“中古风”家具的主力消费群：看看West Elm（美国面向年轻客户群体的高端宜家）这样的零售商里面卖的家具你就知道了。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f355f4582aed5e5d1f82f03b8e250dc5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1074\" data-rawheight=\"520\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1074\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f355f4582aed5e5d1f82f03b8e250dc5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1074&#39; height=&#39;520&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1074\" data-rawheight=\"520\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1074\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f355f4582aed5e5d1f82f03b8e250dc5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f355f4582aed5e5d1f82f03b8e250dc5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>另外，在世界的另一边，中古风家具的主要生产品牌Knoll在今年年初的时候进军中国。所以说，本小编看中古风并未死，而是经过岁月沉淀后，以新的形式更加浩浩荡荡的渗透入了世界主流文化。就如这些被碰红的设计师的初衷一样：<b>大家都能买得起的设计才是好设计。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6c9b936ac07913276242294572bf96a9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"727\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6c9b936ac07913276242294572bf96a9_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;727&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"727\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6c9b936ac07913276242294572bf96a9_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6c9b936ac07913276242294572bf96a9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf0f5e35cc1f2523b276d45075a95ca5_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf0f5e35cc1f2523b276d45075a95ca5_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf0f5e35cc1f2523b276d45075a95ca5_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-cf0f5e35cc1f2523b276d45075a95ca5_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中古风格&#34;Midcentury modern&#34;本身是一个很难定义的词，其实它指向的是20世纪中叶（大概从1933年到1965年）的建筑，室内，家具和平面设计的风格。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>得益于20世纪初的工业革命，设计师们可以运用像塑料这样现在被人百般诟病的新材料；两次世界大战打破原来阶级差距巨大的传统社会制度，设计师们放飞对未来的生活的幻想，设计出这些<b>线条流畅简洁，美观而实用</b>的室内和家具，<b>服务于二战后产生的社会新阶级：中产阶级。</b></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f503f301b28756687b8114f09c620490_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"776\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f503f301b28756687b8114f09c620490_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;776&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"776\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f503f301b28756687b8114f09c620490_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f503f301b28756687b8114f09c620490_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中古风格属于那个国家？有趣的是那些神一般的中古风格设计师们大多是来自战乱的欧洲，而原先属于包豪斯的阵营。二战后，中古风格在美国随着强劲的内需而生根发芽。<b>所以我们可以说中古风格是一个美式风格？Maybe.</b>事实上，二战以后的美国就是一个国际最尖端文化大熔炉，美国已经是很弱的一个民族符号了。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5debc7fa03f1fb3893289c5112ff70d0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5debc7fa03f1fb3893289c5112ff70d0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5debc7fa03f1fb3893289c5112ff70d0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5debc7fa03f1fb3893289c5112ff70d0_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-561cfcfc0dbe2b2cd42e29ffaf34b05b_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"391\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-561cfcfc0dbe2b2cd42e29ffaf34b05b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;391&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"391\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-561cfcfc0dbe2b2cd42e29ffaf34b05b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-561cfcfc0dbe2b2cd42e29ffaf34b05b_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 现代主义风格 （art nouveau） 和中古风格 (mid century modern) 柜</p><p>中古风格家具外形典雅，线条简明流畅，灵感好多都源于大自然植物的流畅线条。说到这里好多机智的宝宝们大概会想到，这不就是20世纪初的现代主义（Art Nouveau)嘛？回答正确，但只对了一半。由于服务的阶级对象不同，中古风格去掉了贵族矫情的过度装饰，流线型的轮廓适合大批量工业生产。</p><p>即便是工业生产，当时中古风格家具质量也优于现在的宜家：当时生产的中古家具是用柚木制成的，柚木可是和红木一样的名贵木材。所以说<b>中古家具就是为当时的中产阶级而生：传承传统，拥抱工业时代，幻想未来；结合实用和美观，注重生活品质。</b></p><p>下面一起来看看中古风格典型家具具体长什么样吧！</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac14197e0c3e50b2f474332f38f107c7_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"920\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac14197e0c3e50b2f474332f38f107c7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1000&#39; height=&#39;920&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1000\" data-rawheight=\"920\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1000\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac14197e0c3e50b2f474332f38f107c7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ac14197e0c3e50b2f474332f38f107c7_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f6aafe2db3cccc2a3db96f591aa5a26_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"355\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f6aafe2db3cccc2a3db96f591aa5a26_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;600&#39; height=&#39;355&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"600\" data-rawheight=\"355\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"600\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f6aafe2db3cccc2a3db96f591aa5a26_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-3f6aafe2db3cccc2a3db96f591aa5a26_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 纽约沙发</p><p><b>沙发</b>：一般中古风格的沙发长得就是这个样子，形状偏几何，像几块饼干组合在一起。上图是一款Edward Wormley设计的“纽约沙发”。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7d5c8e4d2fe7f5fcb3e18588c8d178ac_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"315\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7d5c8e4d2fe7f5fcb3e18588c8d178ac_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;480&#39; height=&#39;315&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"480\" data-rawheight=\"315\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"480\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7d5c8e4d2fe7f5fcb3e18588c8d178ac_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-7d5c8e4d2fe7f5fcb3e18588c8d178ac_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ George Nelson设计的模块组合柜</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c5db893744a14df013ca6674700a6985_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"820\" data-rawheight=\"636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"820\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c5db893744a14df013ca6674700a6985_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;820&#39; height=&#39;636&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"820\" data-rawheight=\"636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"820\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c5db893744a14df013ca6674700a6985_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c5db893744a14df013ca6674700a6985_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ 著名的Cado System 至今还能在北欧设计中找到它的影子</p><p><b>组合柜：</b>模块式墙面组合柜也是中古家具的一大块。设计师追求设计一种模块概念的家具，这样用户就可以按各自己的需求和喜好随意组合，做到以模块应万变。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4ad7298e7b0613eda1ab2e74d3bbf312_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"476\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"476\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4ad7298e7b0613eda1ab2e74d3bbf312_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;476&#39; height=&#39;640&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"476\" data-rawheight=\"640\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"476\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4ad7298e7b0613eda1ab2e74d3bbf312_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4ad7298e7b0613eda1ab2e74d3bbf312_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>坐具：</b>椅子是中古风最高产的家具种类了吧！各位宝宝大概听说过这些如雷贯耳的名字：Eames夫妇，EeroSaarinen，Harry Bertoia，Arne Jacobsen… 这些椅子很显著的共同特征就是由于技术进步，新材料制造曲线更加便利，所以除了美观，新型椅子更加能够贴合人体曲线。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-801883a41db54896c506d6d4fcf42c15_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1320\" data-rawheight=\"747\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1320\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-801883a41db54896c506d6d4fcf42c15_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1320&#39; height=&#39;747&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1320\" data-rawheight=\"747\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1320\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-801883a41db54896c506d6d4fcf42c15_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-801883a41db54896c506d6d4fcf42c15_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>灯具</b>：中古最有名的设计要数Isamu Noguchi的Akari纸灯雕塑系列和由朝鲜蓟为启发灵感的吊灯。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0e341c270bfff50e603fc8114c915224_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"718\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0e341c270bfff50e603fc8114c915224_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;718&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"718\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0e341c270bfff50e603fc8114c915224_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0e341c270bfff50e603fc8114c915224_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><b>屏风：</b>左边是Eileen Gray的大漆屏风，通过折叠打开可以组成不同开合效果。右边是用当时蒸汽新技术使木头变成这种曲面的屏风。</p><p><b>壁纸：</b>颜色鲜艳的几何形体的壁纸是中古风格的特征。我想说，虽然至今还有人用着中古家具，但是很少人敢用这样的墙纸。原因是它们太抢镜了，搭配不好会被人嘲笑玩超越。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p>说超越就超越……………</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-096aeb768feff519da199fda4c02eeff_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"850\" data-rawheight=\"1830\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"850\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-096aeb768feff519da199fda4c02eeff_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;850&#39; height=&#39;1830&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"850\" data-rawheight=\"1830\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"850\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-096aeb768feff519da199fda4c02eeff_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-096aeb768feff519da199fda4c02eeff_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1d8c37dde37bb6fbd6ec5bb0024cee1_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1d8c37dde37bb6fbd6ec5bb0024cee1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;2331&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2331\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"2331\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1d8c37dde37bb6fbd6ec5bb0024cee1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a1d8c37dde37bb6fbd6ec5bb0024cee1_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果你宝宝一直活在广告狂人的梦中，那你一定希望把家里装成中古风格。中古家具现在在市面上存在的方式有：古董，假古董，同款再生产，改良版生产(比如宜家和淘宝)。</p><p>先撇开古董和假古董，我们来说说其他途径。同款再生产的牌子有：赫曼米勒（HERMAN MILLER),Knoll,Vitra。这些品牌都是当年和设计师们签约的公司，如今他们都进入了中国，只是在国内销售的款式比国外要少很多,价格也会相对较高。一把Eames 木质底座模压胶合板休闲座椅的价格在一万到一万五千之间。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8021f4c5deeed0301296b9c503bc9df9_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"321\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"400\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;400&#39; height=&#39;321&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"400\" data-rawheight=\"321\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"400\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-8021f4c5deeed0301296b9c503bc9df9_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>△ Eames 木质底座模压胶合板休闲座椅 </p><p>淘宝上其实也有些中古风格家具改良版/高仿版店。趁着双十一，给大家推荐两个做的规模还挺大的店。<b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//item.taobao.com/item.htm%3Fspm%3Da230r.1.14.55.3c2d5c9ajfJ6Xr%26id%3D552915202880%26ns%3D1%26abbucket%3D12%23detail\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">丹瑞万象进口古董家具</a></b>，这是一个古董+海淘中古风家具的店。另一个是<b><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//norhor.tmall.com/shop/view_shop.htm%3Fspm%3Da230r.1.14.13.62b2273bLmfizn%26user_number_id%3D1646324413\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Norhor旗舰店</a></b>(特别是堪培拉系列)，这个则是改良高仿版专卖店，做的规模还挺大，木质家具是他们家特长。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-18a74bd687366fec223d90bba944501e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"791\" data-rawheight=\"462\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"791\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-18a74bd687366fec223d90bba944501e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;791&#39; height=&#39;462&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"791\" data-rawheight=\"462\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"791\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-18a74bd687366fec223d90bba944501e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-18a74bd687366fec223d90bba944501e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>我想说除了家具以外，配色很重要，中古风格也有惯用的色卡: 用上两个下面的撞色，家里直接会被复古。不信看看下面的色彩浓重的中古室内。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fc8183429a4ada205a70425c3ea16afb_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1286\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fc8183429a4ada205a70425c3ea16afb_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;960&#39; height=&#39;1286&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"960\" data-rawheight=\"1286\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"960\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fc8183429a4ada205a70425c3ea16afb_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-fc8183429a4ada205a70425c3ea16afb_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>下面这张图片是中古风格和当代风格的室内对比，大家能一眼看出，其实一眼望过去差就差在色调上。似乎说到中古风格，大家脑子里就出现了芥末黄的沙发和撞色。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ecd4f84fa194154d74328aa7db4c4b73_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"384\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ecd4f84fa194154d74328aa7db4c4b73_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;768&#39; height=&#39;384&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"768\" data-rawheight=\"384\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"768\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ecd4f84fa194154d74328aa7db4c4b73_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ecd4f84fa194154d74328aa7db4c4b73_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果不想那么那么复古，还有一种办法就是中古风格和当代风格结合。小面积的使用撞色，或是下本钱买一两件能给空间定基调的中古家具，然后一点点延伸搭配，也不失为一个好办法。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd76ad1cdb0923611684b00c222783fa_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1500\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd76ad1cdb0923611684b00c222783fa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1500&#39; height=&#39;1000&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1500\" data-rawheight=\"1000\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1500\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd76ad1cdb0923611684b00c222783fa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fd76ad1cdb0923611684b00c222783fa_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>中古风设计还没死？这只能说这些设计的经典和世界中产阶级的队伍的壮大。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>治愈家</b></p><p>一个治愈系的室内设计生活杂志</p><p>绿色|文艺|国际|实用</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;750&#39; height=&#39;670&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"750\" data-rawheight=\"670\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"750\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7173e34406f6ba7207aff4366dff3812_b.jpg\"/></figure><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=http%3A//weixin.qq.com/r/DS6-pxvEmkblrV-E93sf\" class=\" external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\"><span class=\"invisible\">http://</span><span class=\"visible\">weixin.qq.com/r/DS6-pxv</span><span class=\"invisible\">EmkblrV-E93sf</span><span class=\"ellipsis\"></span></a> (二维码自动识别)</p><p></p><p></p>",

            "title": "风格实验室|光线涂色的家", 
            "content": "<figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6e5b2ccf5629148c8510845954b9a28_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1191\" data-rawheight=\"785\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1191\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6e5b2ccf5629148c8510845954b9a28_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1191&#39; height=&#39;785&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1191\" data-rawheight=\"785\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1191\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6e5b2ccf5629148c8510845954b9a28_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b6e5b2ccf5629148c8510845954b9a28_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>大家好，我是一名丹麦设计师，我叫Caroline Feiffer。今天带大家参观我在丹麦市中心的家。平常的工作压力大，家对我来说是一个放松和充电的地方，<b>我希望我的居住环境滋养我的精神世界</b>，所以在设计时选用了淡淡的暖色调，另外家具的购置虽说还不算是断舍离，也是精挑细选，让家里留出足够多的空间，达到让我安静下来的目的。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b326fb593137de45227495da33ebe41c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"960\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b326fb593137de45227495da33ebe41c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;960&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"960\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b326fb593137de45227495da33ebe41c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b326fb593137de45227495da33ebe41c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>整个屋子的木结构都被我们刷出了<b>偏白色</b>，搭配白墙，浅浅勾画出建筑的木结构之美。整个空间也被包围在一片柔和的气氛中。挑选房子的时候，我们特别注重了房屋的光照，斜切的大面积窗户，即使在全年光照不足的北欧，我们的小窝都披满了阳光。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42a379388469b283197b09abfe1ddbaf_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42a379388469b283197b09abfe1ddbaf_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1619&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42a379388469b283197b09abfe1ddbaf_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-42a379388469b283197b09abfe1ddbaf_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>客厅的沙发选用了Gervasoni家的“ghost sofa”, 卧室里的床也是选用这个幽灵系列的，它们柔软得让人想直直地陷到它们的怀抱里，再也不要爬起来。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66021dda9058e46d387ffa3cf364915a_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"952\" data-rawheight=\"932\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"952\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66021dda9058e46d387ffa3cf364915a_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;952&#39; height=&#39;932&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"952\" data-rawheight=\"932\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"952\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66021dda9058e46d387ffa3cf364915a_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-66021dda9058e46d387ffa3cf364915a_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>如果你看到👆图，就能发现这款沙发和中古风格的沙发（左下）截然不同：没有骨架，不平整，没有厚厚的潜入式靠背，反而用褶皱的面料，可移动的抱枕来代替。这种随性而舒适的风格让这款幽灵沙发一上市便红遍一时，算是现代反潮流沙发的一个经典。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-77fdd14bb39911e104ac6ddc002a905e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-77fdd14bb39911e104ac6ddc002a905e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;2197&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-77fdd14bb39911e104ac6ddc002a905e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-77fdd14bb39911e104ac6ddc002a905e_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>说到舒适和放松，最放松的地方当然是卧室了。整个环境我们都用了<b>同色系</b>，少些兴奋和刺激，多些柔和和安静。屋内的<b>家具都是形体粗旷，线条简单</b>，床上用品也选择粗麻材质，而阳光则给了空间神一般的开示。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae3d2d63c66a25d45636f1aa22b5f72c_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"769\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae3d2d63c66a25d45636f1aa22b5f72c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;769&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"769\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae3d2d63c66a25d45636f1aa22b5f72c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ae3d2d63c66a25d45636f1aa22b5f72c_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>纸质灯罩的灯有种东方的韵味，家里几处都选用了Akari和纸纸灯。如今这种随处可见的宜家纸灯，当时横空出世时一举拿下5项美国专利和31项日本专利。除了“可折叠的”纸艺雕塑的艺术价值以外，<b>Akari系列灯具拥有一种难以言表的温馨感</b>，是点缀居所的不二良选。设计师Noguchi曾说过这么一句著名的话：“只要一间屋子、一张榻榻米和一盏Akari，这便有了家的样子。”</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc59b3ec35a431c8706d0e0a20b342be_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc59b3ec35a431c8706d0e0a20b342be_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1619&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1619\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc59b3ec35a431c8706d0e0a20b342be_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fc59b3ec35a431c8706d0e0a20b342be_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>厨房当然要面朝阳光。一改西方的布艺窗帘，我们选用了东方的竹帘。你们喜欢<b>古董</b>吗？我对古董有着特殊的情感，它们比新的器物更加润，好像一个成熟的能量，帮助你卸去浮躁。这张餐桌就是网上淘的法国古董，下午阳光好时，也能在这里做着喝茶看书。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ecbda90562b1326f66ba823eebd6b8de_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ecbda90562b1326f66ba823eebd6b8de_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1080&#39; height=&#39;1636&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1080\" data-rawheight=\"1636\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1080\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ecbda90562b1326f66ba823eebd6b8de_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-ecbda90562b1326f66ba823eebd6b8de_b.jpg\"/></figure><p>厨房里的一些<b>收纳我们做了开放式的处理</b>。好多器皿都是我们精心挑选的，无论从颜色上还是材质上都非常搭配，放在一起本身就是一副美丽的画卷，收纳在里面就可惜了。<br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6ae6387ea43754970d2fc0f1e49ad676_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6ae6387ea43754970d2fc0f1e49ad676_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;978&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"978\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6ae6387ea43754970d2fc0f1e49ad676_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6ae6387ea43754970d2fc0f1e49ad676_b.jpg\"/></figure><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87ec040939148a5fa26adab59418a2f0_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87ec040939148a5fa26adab59418a2f0_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1466&#39; height=&#39;2197&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"1466\" data-rawheight=\"2197\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1466\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87ec040939148a5fa26adab59418a2f0_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-87ec040939148a5fa26adab59418a2f0_b.jpg\"/></figure><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-91daa4c0c8eab75c41c74a1795d505dd_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"2475\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"2475\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-91daa4c0c8eab75c41c74a1795d505dd_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
